namespace = gene_pillars

#0-99 - System events
#100-199 - Kiamoa Pillar events        (Used: 100, 101-106, 111-117, 121-128)
#200-299 - Mechanim Pillar events      (Used: 200, 211-218, 221-227, 231-238)
#300-399 - Hinuifauna Pillar events    (Used: 300, 311-315, 321-327, 331-337)
#400-499 - Holohana Pillar events      (Used: 400, 411-416, 421-428, 431-438)
#500-599 - Forest Pillar events        (Used: 500, 511-521, 531-538, 541-547)
#600-699 - Collection Pillar events    (Used: 600, 601-606, 611-617, 621-629)
#700-799 - Kraken Pillar events        (Used: 700, 711-715, 721-727, 731-737)
#800-899 - Sandworm Pillar events      (Used: 800, 811-820, 821-832, 833-846)
#900-999 - Dragon Pillar events        (Used: 900, 911-915, 921-926, 931-937)
#1000+ - Generic exploration events    (Used: 1000, 1002-1019, 1050-1059)
#99999 - Debug event

#INFO ABOUT HOW TO MAKE MORE EVENTS

#Immediately in every event, you must set the gene_pillars_has_pending_event country flag,
#and then remove it in the after, otherwise ending the expedition will not work.

#Passive Study
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.0
	title = gene_pillars.0.t
	desc = gene_pillars.0.d
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Give invention
	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.0.a
		gene_pillars_random_insyaa_invention_unlock = yes
	}
}

#Start or turn back
province_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.2
	title = gene_pillars.2.t
	desc = gene_pillars.2.d
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			owner = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
			save_event_target_as = gene_pillar_exploration_province
		}
	}

	#Let's Go!
	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.2.a
		hidden_effect = {
			add_province_triggered_modifier = gene_pillar_exploration_randomness_ptm
			gene_pillars_set_class_flags_on_country_effect = yes

			# clear_setup_flags = yes #what should be done about this time, for most of them at least
			remove_province_modifier = gene_pillars_next_level_extra_1_hp
		}
	}
	
	#Actually, I changed my mind.
	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.2.b
		hidden_effect = {
			owner = {
				clr_country_flag = aPUI_gene_pillar_is_exploring_3376
				clr_country_flag = aPUI_gene_pillar_is_exploring_3415
				clr_country_flag = aPUI_gene_pillar_is_exploring_3329
				clr_country_flag = aPUI_gene_pillar_is_exploring_3173
				clr_country_flag = aPUI_gene_pillar_is_exploring_3153
				clr_country_flag = aPUI_gene_pillar_is_exploring_6950
				clr_country_flag = aPUI_gene_pillar_is_exploring_6962
				clr_country_flag = aPUI_gene_pillar_is_exploring_3551
				clr_country_flag = aPUI_gene_pillar_is_exploring_6386
				clr_country_flag = gene_pillar_is_exploring_level_1_pillar
				clr_country_flag = gene_pillar_is_exploring_level_2_pillar
				clr_country_flag = gene_pillar_is_exploring_level_3_pillar
			}
		}
	}

	after = { hidden_effect = { owner = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } } }
}

#Abandon exploration province
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.3
	title = none
	desc = none
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes
	immediate = {
		gene_pillar_abandon_expedition_effect_helper = { province = yes }
	}
	option = {
		name = none
	}
}

#Level up notification
province_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.6
	title = gene_pillars.6.t
	desc = gene_pillars.6.d
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.6.a
		tooltip = { change_variable = { which = aPUI_gene_pillars_party_level_var_dummy value = 1 } }
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { owner = { has_country_modifier = mechanim_administration } } }
			if = {
				limit = { owner = { gene_pillars_is_exactly_party_level = { level = 3 } } }
				custom_tooltip = gene_pillars_unlock_classes_level_3_tt
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { owner = { gene_pillars_is_exactly_party_level = { level = 4 } } }
				custom_tooltip = gene_pillars_unlock_classes_level_4_tt
			}
		}
	}
}

#Pillar ends successfully
province_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.30
	title = gene_pillars.30.t
	desc = gene_pillars.30.d
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		#This one is free as a reward
		hidden_effect = { gene_pillars_randomise_loot_event = yes }
	}

	#Get Loot
	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.30.a

		# If anyone is injured, show it in the tooltip
		gene_pillars_injury_check_tooltips = yes
		# # If you have 100 loot, subtract 100. Do it here so the customisable loc works
		# TODO make the loc work properly since you're gaining rewards during the expedition now
		# gene_pillars_check_loot_threshold = yes
		# Finishing a pillar always gives loot
		gene_pillars_gain_final_loot_event = yes
		# Get the T4 invention
		owner = { gene_pillars_T4_invention_unlock = yes }

		hidden_effect = {
			# TODO: hacky - we have to clear the XP and Loot here as you can see the expedition window again if you hold the finishing events open
			# but we also need to update XP again in each completion event, because you might level up and change your XP again
			# and you may have maxed your Loot, thereby resetting it
			# improve this
			owner = { aPUI_gene_pillar_update_all_gene_pillar_progress_bars = yes }
		}
	}
}

		# # If you have 100 loot, fire the gene_pillars_randomise_loot_event with a tooltip
		# gene_pillars_check_loot_threshold = yes

		hidden_effect = {
			# TODO: hacky - we have to clear the XP and Loot here as you can see the expedition window again if you hold the finishing events open
			# but we also need to update XP again in each completion event, because you might level up and change your XP again
			# and you may have maxed your Loot, thereby resetting it
			# improve this
			owner = { aPUI_gene_pillar_update_all_gene_pillar_progress_bars = yes }
		}
	}
}

#Pillar ends in failure (but on country scope, so on_action works fine)
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.32
	title = gene_pillars.31.t
	desc = gene_pillars.32.d
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.31.a

		event_target:gene_pillar_exploration_province = {
			# If anyone is injured, show it in the tooltip
			gene_pillars_injury_check_tooltips = yes
			# TODO we need to make loot work when you abandon - if you had 100, gain a reward
			# # If you have 100 loot, fire the gene_pillars_randomise_loot_event with a tooltip
			# gene_pillars_check_loot_threshold = yes
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			# TODO: hacky - we have to clear the XP and Loot here as you can see the expedition window again if you hold the finishing events open
			# but we also need to update XP again in each completion event, because you might level up and change your XP again
			# and you may have maxed your Loot, thereby resetting it
			# improve this
			aPUI_gene_pillar_update_all_gene_pillar_progress_bars = yes
		}
	}
}

#Gain a reward for 100 loot
province_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.33
	title = gene_pillars.33.t
	desc = gene_pillars.33.d
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { gene_pillars_randomise_loot_event = { looted = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.33.a

		gene_pillars_gain_final_loot_event = yes
	}
}

#Get Precursor Relics
province_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.40
	title = gene_pillars.40.t
	desc = gene_pillars.40.d
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Get Permanent Precursor Relics
	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.40.a
		save_trade_goods = yes
		change_trade_goods = precursor_relics
	}

	#Get  Precursor Relics
	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.40.b
		save_trade_goods = yes
		change_trade_goods = precursor_relics
		province_event = { id = gene_pillars.41 days = 7300 random = 7300 }
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_rich_precursor_relics
			duration = -1
		}
	}
}

#Lose Precursor Relics
province_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.41
	title = gene_pillars.41.t
	desc = gene_pillars.41.d
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Lose Precursor Relics
	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.41.a
		set_from_saved_trade_goods = yes
		remove_province_modifier = gene_pillars_rich_precursor_relics
	}
}

#Get Damestear
province_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.50
	title = gene_pillars.50.t
	desc = gene_pillars.50.d
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Get Damestear
	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.50.a
		save_trade_goods = yes
		change_trade_goods = damestear
		set_province_flag = summoned_damestear
		province_event = { id = damestear.5 days = 7300 random = 7300 }
		add_province_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_rich_damestear
			duration = -1
		}
	}
}

#Ai get institutions
province_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.67
	title = gene_pillars.67.t
	desc = gene_pillars.67.d
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.67.a
		gene_pillars = {
			limit = {
				owner = {
					ai = yes
					NOT = {
						is_mechanim_tribe = yes
						government = native
					}
				}
				is_city = yes
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				area = {
					limit = { is_city = yes }
					add_next_institution_embracement = 50
					add_permanent_province_modifier = {
						name = gene_pillars_ai_institutions
						duration = 3650 #10 years
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

#Setup events
##Unlock initial classes
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.90
	title = gene_pillars.90.t
	desc = gene_pillars.90.d
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_modifier = mechanim_administration } }
			set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_rogue_A
			set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_ranger_A
			set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_fighter_A
			set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_cleric_A
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_not_banned_magic_artificery = yes
				}
				if = {
					limit = { insyaa_has_flamesong = yes }
					set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_mage_B
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { insyaa_has_wavesong = yes }
					set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_mage_C
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { insyaa_has_stonescrawl = yes }
					set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_mage_D
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { insyaa_has_stonestory = yes }
					set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_mage_E
				}
				else = {
					set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_mage_A
				}
			}
			if = {
				limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = magic_artificery_mage_only } }
				set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_artificer_A
			}
		}
		else = {
			set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_rogue_D
			set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_rogue_E
			set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_ranger_E
			set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_fighter_E
			set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_cleric_E
			set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_artificer_E
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.90.a
		#Leave empty, use the immediate
	}
}

#Clear class flags for slot
province_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.93
	title = gene_pillars.93.t
	desc = gene_pillars.93.d
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	immediate = {
		trigger_switch = {
			on_trigger = has_province_flag
			gene_pillars_selecting_slot_1 = { gene_pillars_setup_clear_party_slot = { slot = 1 } }
			gene_pillars_selecting_slot_2 = { gene_pillars_setup_clear_party_slot = { slot = 2 } }
			gene_pillars_selecting_slot_3 = { gene_pillars_setup_clear_party_slot = { slot = 3 } }
			gene_pillars_selecting_slot_4 = { gene_pillars_setup_clear_party_slot = { slot = 4 } }
			gene_pillars_selecting_slot_5 = { gene_pillars_setup_clear_party_slot = { slot = 5 } }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.93.a
	}
}


#Use in on_province_owner_change and elsewhere to reset the province
province_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.94
	title = gene_pillars.99.t
	desc = gene_pillars.99.d
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.100.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = { is_empty = yes }
				owner = {
					exists = yes
					has_country_flag = aPUI_gene_pillar_interaction_setup_done
				}
			}
			clr_province_flag = aPUI_gene_pillar_interaction_setup_done_province
			aPUI_gene_pillar_setup_province = yes
		}
	}
}

#Fire this to abandon exploration for owner
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.98
	title = gene_pillars.98.t
	desc = gene_pillars.98.d
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		aPUI_clear_all_province_exploration_flags = yes
		FROM = { aPUI_clear_all_country_exploration_flags = yes }
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.98.a
	}
}

#Kiamoa Pillar events
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.100
	title = gene_pillars.100.t
	desc = gene_pillars.100.d
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	# immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }
	#Next event
	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.100.a
		trigger_switch = {
			on_trigger = has_country_flag
			gene_pillar_is_exploring_level_1_pillar = {
				gene_pillars_set_up_progress_bar = { events = 10 }
				gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 101 }
			}
			gene_pillar_is_exploring_level_2_pillar = {
				gene_pillars_set_up_progress_bar = { events = 12 }
				gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 111 }
			}
			gene_pillar_is_exploring_level_3_pillar = {
				gene_pillars_set_up_progress_bar = { events = 14 }
				gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 121 }
			}
		}
	}
	# after = { hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }
}

### Kiamoa Pillar Level 1
# A Fault in the Delve
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.101
	title = gene_pillars.101.t
	desc = gene_pillars.101.d
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }
	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.101.a
		random = {
			chance = 75
			gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.101.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_rogue_in_party = yes
				gene_pillars_has_sentry_mechanim_in_party = yes
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		random = {
			chance = 50
			gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.101.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_stonescrawl_mage_in_party = yes

	}

	}

#Mechanim Pillar events
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.200
	title = gene_pillars.200.t
	desc = gene_pillars.200.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	# immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	#Next event
	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.200.a
		
		# gene_pillars_check_extra_hp_at_start = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = gene_pillar_is_exploring_level_1_pillar
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				gene_pillars_set_up_progress_bar = { events = 10 }
			}
			gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 211 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = gene_pillar_is_exploring_level_2_pillar
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				gene_pillars_set_up_progress_bar = { events = 12 }
			}
			gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 221 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = gene_pillar_is_exploring_level_3_pillar
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				gene_pillars_set_up_progress_bar = { events = 14 }

# The Great Furnace
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.217
	title = gene_pillars.217.t
	desc = gene_pillars.217.d
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # Not good
		name = gene_pillars.217.a

		gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 }
	}

	option = { # Break through
		name = gene_pillars.217.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_barbarian_in_party = yes
				gene_pillars_has_earthsculptor_mechanim_in_party = yes
			}			
		}
		highlight = yes
		
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 }
			}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 3 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # passage up there
		name = gene_pillars.217.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_modifier = harpy_administration
				gene_pillars_has_soarer_mechanim_in_party = yes
			}			
		}
		highlight = yes
		
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 }
			}
			3 = {}
		}
	}

	option = { # Bend the fire
		name = gene_pillars.217.e
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = mage }
					gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 2 }
				}
				gene_pillars_has_flamesong_mage_in_party = yes
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
	}
	
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event
			country_event = {
				id = gene_pillars.218
			}
		}
	}
}

### Mechanim Pillar Level 2
# Back Again
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.221
	title = gene_pillars.221.t
	desc = gene_pillars.221.d
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # Didn’t quite catch that
		name = gene_pillars.221.a
		trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_modifier = elven_administration
					has_country_modifier = half_elven_administration
					has_country_modifier = ruinborn_administration
				}
			}
		}

		gene_pillars_lose_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = { # Alright, got it  
		name = gene_pillars.221.b
		trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_modifier = elven_administration
					has_country_modifier = half_elven_administration
					has_country_modifier = ruinborn_administration
				}
			}
			OR = {
				has_country_modifier = mechanim_administration
				gene_pillars_has_any_mechanim_in_party = yes
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = { # How many curses was that
		name = gene_pillars.221.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_modifier = elven_administration
				has_country_modifier = half_elven_administration
				has_country_modifier = ruinborn_administration
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_lose_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
	}

	option = { # got a spell for this
		name = gene_pillars.221.e
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = mage }
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 2 }
			has_mana = { amount = 10 }
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_modifier = elven_administration
					has_country_modifier = half_elven_administration
					has_country_modifier = ruinborn_administration
				}
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		change_mana = { amount = -10 }
		add_adm_power = 25
		add_dip_power = 25
		add_mil_power = 25
	}
	
	after = {	
		gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 222 advance = yes }
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
	}
}

		}
		highlight = yes

	}

		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
	}

		highlight = yes

			3 = {}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # reason with them 
		name = gene_pillars.225.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_modifier = mechanim_administration
				medium_tolerance_mechanim_race_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		
		add_dip_power = -20
		random_list = {
			3 = {}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # draw them out
		name = gene_pillars.225.e
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_soarer_mechanim_in_party = yes
		}
		highlight = yes
		
		gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 15 }
	}
	
	after = {	
		gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 226 advance = yes }
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
	}

# Target Spotted
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.232
	title = gene_pillars.232.t
	desc = gene_pillars.232.d
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # try not to get hit
		name = gene_pillars.232.a
		trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_modifier = elven_administration
					has_country_modifier = half_elven_administration
					has_country_modifier = ruinborn_administration
				}
			}
		}

		gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_lose_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = { # alert them to your location  
		name = gene_pillars.232.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				has_country_modifier = elven_administration
				has_country_modifier = half_elven_administration
				has_country_modifier = ruinborn_administration
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		gene_pillars_lose_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
	}

	option = { # must have damestear
		name = gene_pillars.232.c
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 2 }
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_modifier = elven_administration
					has_country_modifier = half_elven_administration
					has_country_modifier = ruinborn_administration
				}
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 15 }
		
	}

	option = { # easy to trick
		name = gene_pillars.232.e
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = mage }
					gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 2 }
				}
				gene_pillars_has_wavesong_mage_in_party = yes
			}
			has_mana = { amount = 10 }
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_modifier = elven_administration
					has_country_modifier = half_elven_administration
					has_country_modifier = ruinborn_administration
				}
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 4 }
		change_mana = { amount = -10 }
	}

	option = { # Stay low
		name = gene_pillars.232.f
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = rogue }
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 2 }
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_modifier = elven_administration
					has_country_modifier = half_elven_administration
					has_country_modifier = ruinborn_administration
				}
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		add_dip_power = 15
		random_list = {
			3 = {}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 }
			}
		}
	}
	
	after = {	
		gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 233 advance = yes }
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
	}
}

# A Million Faces
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.236
	title = gene_pillars.236.t
	desc = gene_pillars.236.d
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # get them above ground
		name = gene_pillars.236.a
		trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_modifier = mechanim_administration
				}
			}
		}

		random_province = {
			limit = {
				owned_by = ROOT
				NOT = { has_dormant_mechanim = yes }
			}
			add_permanent_province_modifier = { name = dormant_mechanim duration = -1 }
		}
	}

	option = { # welcome them to their new home
		name = gene_pillars.236.b
		trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				has_country_modifier = mechanim_administration
			}
		}

		ROOT = {
			capital_scope = {
				add_base_tax = 1
				add_base_production = 1
				add_base_manpower = 1
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # end their dormancy
		name = gene_pillars.236.c
		trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_modifier = mechanim_administration
				}
			}
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 2 }
		}
		highlight = yes

		random_province = {
			limit = {
				owned_by = ROOT
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_large_mechanim_minority_trigger = yes
				}
				add_random_development = 1
			}
			add_mechanim_large_minority_effect = yes
		}
	}

	option = { # We can teach
		name = gene_pillars.236.e
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_domestic_mechanim_in_party = yes
		}
		highlight = yes

		add_dip_power = 25
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = mechanim_administration
			}
			ROOT = {
				capital_scope = {
					add_base_tax = 1
					add_base_production = 1
					add_base_manpower = 1
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			large_increase_of_mechanim_tolerance_effect = yes
			random_province = {
				limit = {
					owned_by = ROOT
					NOT = {
						has_large_mechanim_minority_trigger = yes
						has_small_mechanim_minority_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				add_mechanim_large_minority_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # never really alive
		name = gene_pillars.236.f
		trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_modifier = mechanim_administration
				}
			}
		}

		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 25 }
		largest_decrease_of_mechanim_tolerance_effect = yes
		every_known_country = {
			limit = {
				culture_group = mechanim
			}
			add_opinion = {
				who = ROOT
				modifier = gene_pillars_mechanim_dismantled_mechanim
			}
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 237 advance = yes }
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
	}
}

		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_warrior_mechanim_in_party = yes
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 3 }
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		add_mil_power = 25
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 15 }
	}
	
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event
			country_event = {
				id = gene_pillars.238
			}
		}
	}
}

		name = gene_pillars.300.a

		# gene_pillars_check_extra_hp_at_start = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = gene_pillar_is_exploring_level_1_pillar
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				gene_pillars_set_up_progress_bar = { events = 12 }
			}
			gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 311 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = gene_pillar_is_exploring_level_2_pillar
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				gene_pillars_set_up_progress_bar = { events = 14 }
			}
			gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 321 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = gene_pillar_is_exploring_level_3_pillar
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				gene_pillars_set_up_progress_bar = { events = 14 }
			}
			gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 331 }
		}
	}
	
	# #I've had enough of this wild ride
	# option = {
	# 	name = gene_pillars.300.b
	# 	gene_pillar_end_expedition_effect = yes
	# }

	# after = { hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }
}

	desc = gene_pillars.311.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture

	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province

		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.311.a

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.311.b

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 4 }
		random = {
			chance = 25
			gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.311.c
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = ranger }
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 3 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.311.d
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = mage }
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 3 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.311.e
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_stonescrawl_mage_in_party = yes
				gene_pillars_has_stonestory_mage_in_party = yes
				gene_pillars_has_earthsculptor_mechanim_in_party = yes
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 3 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
		gene_pillars_add_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 312 advance = yes }
	}
}

		gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 4 }
		add_prestige = 20		
	}

	option = { # Fight it together and learn
		name = gene_pillars.323.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_paladin_in_party = yes
				gene_pillars_has_amount_of_archetype_in_party = { amount = 2 archetype = fighter }
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		random = {
			chance = 10
			gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 3 }
		add_mil_power = 50
	}

	option = { # Use salves and learn

		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = cleric }
		}
		highlight = yes

		random = {
			chance = 10
			gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 3 }
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_orange_manpower_recovery_10_salves
			duration = 3650 # 10 years
		}
	}

	option = { # Evade it and tire it out
		name = gene_pillars.323.e
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_amount_of_archetype_in_party = { amount = 2 archetype = ranger }
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 15 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 20 }
	}

	after = {

		gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 324 advance = yes }

# Hinuispiders
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.324
	title = gene_pillars.324.t
	desc = gene_pillars.324.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # Get as much info as possible
		name = gene_pillars.324.a

		gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 20 }
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 4 }
	}

	option = { # We're not here for spiders
		name = gene_pillars.324.b

		random = {
			chance = 50
			gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = { # Tread carefully
		name = gene_pillars.324.c
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = ranger }
		}
		highlight = yes

		random = {
			chance = 10
			gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
	}

	option = { # Counter the poison
		name = gene_pillars.324.d
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = cleric }
		}
		highlight = yes

		random = {
			chance = 10
			gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
	}

	option = { # Imagine worrying about poison...
		name = gene_pillars.324.e
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_all_mechanim_party_country = yes
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 20 }
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 325 advance = yes }
	}
}

# Hinuiwar - bees and wasps
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.325
	title = gene_pillars.325.t
	desc = gene_pillars.325.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # Run straight through
		name = gene_pillars.325.a

		random = {
			chance = 75
			gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillar_orange_morale_5_suicidal_bravery
			duration = 3650 # 10 years
		}
	}

	option = { # On the ground!
		name = gene_pillars.325.b

		random = {
			chance = 25
			gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillar_orange_move_speed_5_bee_avoidance
			duration = 3650 # 10 years
		}
	}

	option = { # Burn it all out
		name = gene_pillars.325.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_flamesong_mage_in_party = yes
				AND = { # I think this is what he meant
					NOT = {
						capital_scope = {
							continent = oceania
						}
					}
					gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = mage }
				}
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 25 }
		random = {
			chance = 10
			gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 4 }
	}

	option = { # Zap the wasps
		name = gene_pillars.325.d
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = ranger }
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = mage }
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 20 }
	}

	option = { # Shields up!
		name = gene_pillars.325.e
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_any_support_class_country = yes
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = mage }
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 20 }
	}

	option = { # We know how to ally hinuibees
		name = gene_pillars.325.f
		trigger = {
			tag = N42 # Pohaimeli
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 25 }
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 326 advance = yes }
	}
}

# Into the Eyrie
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.327
	title = gene_pillars.327.t
	desc = gene_pillars.327.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # Don't bother
		name = gene_pillars.327.a

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillar_orange_build_time_5_expediency
			duration = 3650 # 10 years
		}
	}

	option = { # Fire and tents
		name = gene_pillars.327.b

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 15 }
	}

	option = { # Auto-firing doodads for defence
		name = gene_pillars.327.c
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 20 }
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		# Next tier events are twice as fast
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_exploration_events_double_speed
	}

	option = { # Set traps
		name = gene_pillars.327.d
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = rogue }
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 20 }
		# Next tier events are twice as fast
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_exploration_events_double_speed
	}

	option = { # Build an earth wall
		name = gene_pillars.327.e
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_stonescrawl_mage_in_party = yes
				gene_pillars_has_stonestory_mage_in_party = yes
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 20 }
		
		event_target:gene_pillar_exploration_province = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = gene_pillars_next_level_extra_1_hp
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Hide supply caches
		name = gene_pillars.327.f
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = ranger }
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 20 }
		
		event_target:gene_pillar_exploration_province = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = gene_pillars_next_level_extra_1_hp
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		gene_pillar_end_expedition_effect = yes
	}
}

# Hinuicrows
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.334
	title = gene_pillars.334.t
	desc = gene_pillars.334.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # Just kill 'em
		name = gene_pillars.334.a

		random = {
			chance = 50
			gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 25 }
		random = {
			chance = 50
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = gene_pillars_orange_stab_10_crow_vendetta
				duration = 3650 # 10 years
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Show we mean no harm
		name = gene_pillars.334.b

		random = {
			chance = 10
			gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = { # Let's trade
		name = gene_pillars.334.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_amount_of_archetype_in_party = { amount = 2 archetype = ranger }
				AND = {
					gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = ranger }
					gene_pillars_has_any_support_class_country = yes
				}
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 4 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 25 }
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_orange_trade_power_5_crows_love_us
			duration = 7300 # 20 years
		}
	}

# Hinuiroo
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.336
	title = gene_pillars.336.t
	desc = gene_pillars.336.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # We are not going to fight that thing
		name = gene_pillars.336.a

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_orange_stab_5_good_sense
			duration = 3650 # 10 years
		}
	}

	option = { # Uh, sure, let's fight
		name = gene_pillars.336.b

		gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 4 }
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_orange_shock_5_boxing
			duration = 7300 # 20 years
		}
	}

	option = { # Hell yeah, let's fight!
		name = gene_pillars.336.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_amount_of_archetype_in_party = { amount = 2 archetype = fighter }
				gene_pillars_has_barbarian_in_party = yes
				gene_pillars_has_paladin_in_party = yes
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 4 }
		random = {
			chance = 50
			gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_orange_shock_5_boxing
			duration = 7300 # 20 years
		}
	}

	option = { # The aggy bastard will run right into our traps
		name = gene_pillars.336.d
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = rogue }
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		add_prestige = 10
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 20 }
	}

	option = { # Let's find a kinder way to play
		name = gene_pillars.336.e
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = ranger }
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 4 }
		random = {
			chance = 10
			gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_orange_shock_received_5_evasion
			duration = 3650 # 10 years
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 337 advance = yes }
	}
}

# Hinuigarkain
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.337
	title = gene_pillars.337.t
	desc = gene_pillars.337.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # A repulsive creature and a threat - kill it
		name = gene_pillars.337.a

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 4 }
		add_prestige = 20
		add_stability = 1
	}

	option = { # Study her, as the Precursors did
		name = gene_pillars.337.b

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 4 }
		event_target:gene_pillar_exploration_province = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = gene_pillars_orange_manpower_recovery_10_restored_gene_lab
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # We can communicate with her peacefully, I know it
		name = gene_pillars.337.c
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_amount_of_archetype_in_party = { amount = 2 archetype = ranger }
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 4 }
		event_target:gene_pillar_exploration_province = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = gene_pillars_orange_hinuifauna_reserve
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # What games the Precursors have played with the soul
		name = gene_pillars.337.d
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_amount_of_mechanim_country = { amount = 3 }
			NOT = { tag = M30 } # I-Numbe
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 4 }
		change_government_reform_progress  = 250
	}

	option = { # She was honoured to serve the Makers.
		name = gene_pillars.337.e
		trigger = {
			tag = M30 # I-Numbe
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 4 }
		event_target:gene_pillar_exploration_province = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = gene_pillars_orange_hallowed_gene_lab
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # This is her home, and she is sentient...
		name = gene_pillars.337.f

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 4 }
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_orange_spirit_of_mercy
			duration = -1
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event
			clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_exploration_events_double_speed
		}
		gene_pillar_end_expedition_effect = yes
	}
}

	title = gene_pillars.400.t
	desc = gene_pillars.400.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	# immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	#Next event
	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.400.a
		
		# gene_pillars_check_extra_hp_at_start = yes
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = gene_pillar_is_exploring_level_1_pillar
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				gene_pillars_set_up_progress_bar = { events = 10 }
			}
			gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 411 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = gene_pillar_is_exploring_level_2_pillar
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				gene_pillars_set_up_progress_bar = { events = 12 }
			}
			gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 421 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = gene_pillar_is_exploring_level_3_pillar
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				gene_pillars_set_up_progress_bar = { events = 14 }
			}
			gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 431 }
		}
	}
}

	option = { # Jewels
		name = gene_pillars.411.a
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				gene_pillars_all_mechanim_party_country = yes
			}
		}

		random_list = {

	}

			NOT = {

			}
		}

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

			NOT = {
				gene_pillars_all_mechanim_party_country = yes
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		random_list = {
			9 = {}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
		}
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }

			gene_pillars_all_mechanim_party_country = yes

	}

country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.421
	title = gene_pillars.421.t
	desc = gene_pillars.421.d
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # Fight through what remains
		name = gene_pillars.421.a

		random_list = {
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 }
				gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # bait them  
		name = gene_pillars.421.b

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
			3 = {}
		}
	}

	option = { # learn from this
		name = gene_pillars.421.c
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = mage }
			is_estate_transmutation_level_1_minimum = yes
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_holohana_ancient_constructs
			duration = 7300
		}
	}

	option = { # Rotten bait
		name = gene_pillars.421.e
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = rogue }
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 2 }
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
	}
	
	after = {	
		gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 422 advance = yes }
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
	}
}

	}

		name = gene_pillars.422.a
	}

	option = { # Squeeze through  
		name = gene_pillars.422.b
		
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
				gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
			}
			1 = {}
		}
	}

	option = { # Burn it to the ground
		name = gene_pillars.422.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = mage }
					is_estate_evocation_level_1_minimum = yes
				}
				gene_pillars_has_flamesong_mage_in_party = yes
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
	}

	option = { # great deterrents
		name = gene_pillars.422.e
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_all_mechanim_party_country = yes
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_holohana_spiked_shells
			duration = 3650
		}
	}
	
	after = {

			}
		}

		}
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_holohana_military_study_flag
	}

	option = { # strive to understand
		name = gene_pillars.427.b
		
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_holohana_diplomatic_study
			duration = 3650
		}
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_holohana_diplomatic_study_flag
	}

	option = { # affect the land
		name = gene_pillars.427.c
		
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_holohana_administrative_study
			duration = 3650
		}
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_holohana_administrative_study_flag
	}

			}

# add upgraded modifier from memory log
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.428
	title = gene_pillars.428.t
	desc = gene_pillars.428.d
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	option = { # focus on the tactics.
		name = gene_pillars.428.a

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = gene_pillars_holohana_military_study_flag
			}
			clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_holohana_military_study_flag
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = gene_pillars_holohana_pack_tactics
				duration = 7300
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = gene_pillars_holohana_diplomatic_study_flag
			}
			clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_holohana_diplomatic_study_flag
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = gene_pillars_holohana_hive_mind
				duration = 7300
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = gene_pillars_holohana_administrative_study_flag
			}
			clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_holohana_administrative_study_flag
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = gene_pillars_holohana_herd_mentality
				duration = 7300
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.434
	title = gene_pillars.434.t
	desc = gene_pillars.434.d
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # Watch out for the sparks
		name = gene_pillars.434.a

		gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = { # memories will guide us
		name = gene_pillars.434.b

		random_list = {
			1 = {}
			3 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 }
				gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Surprisingly refreshing
		name = gene_pillars.434.c
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_all_mechanim_party_country = yes
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_hp_effect = { amount = 1 overheal = yes }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
		
	}

	option = { # attract the sparks
		name = gene_pillars.434.e
		trigger = {
			check_variable = {
				which = aPUI_gene_pillar_loot_var
				value = 20
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_lose_loot_effect = { amount = 20 }
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 3 }
	}

	option = { # memories WILL show us the way
		name = gene_pillars.434.f
		trigger = {
			is_overall_divination_level_2_minimum = yes
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_holohana_past_foresight
			duration = 9125
		}
	}
	
	after = {

	id = gene_pillars.435

	desc = gene_pillars.435.d
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # Snap them out of it
		name = gene_pillars.435.a

		gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = { # Drama queens
		name = gene_pillars.435.b

		gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
	}

	option = { # Look inside yourself

			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = cleric }
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 3 }

		highlight = yes

			name = gene_pillars_holohana_ties_that_bind

		}

		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = fighter }
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 3 }
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 3 }
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_holohana_pull_it_together

		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 3 }

			name = gene_pillars_holohana_give_no_ground
			duration = 9125
		}
	}
	
	after = {	
		gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 436 advance = yes }
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.436
	title = gene_pillars.436.t
	desc = gene_pillars.436.d
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # Get away
		name = gene_pillars.436.a

		gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = { # isn’t this life
		name = gene_pillars.436.b

		random_list = {
			9 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_add_hp_effect = { amount = 1 overheal = yes }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # finally absorb life itself!
		name = gene_pillars.436.c
		trigger = {
			is_overall_necromancy_level_2_minimum = yes
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_hp_effect = { amount = 1 overheal = yes }
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 3 }
		make_spell_free = {
			school = necromancy
			level = 2
			id = speak_with_dead
			next_cast = yes
		}
	}

	option = { # feels like to be alive
		name = gene_pillars.436.e
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_all_mechanim_party_country = yes
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 3 }
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_holohana_pull_youths_energy
			duration = 9125
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 437 advance = yes }
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.437
	title = gene_pillars.437.t
	desc = gene_pillars.437.d
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # But that isn’t me
		name = gene_pillars.437.a

		gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 }
	}

	option = { # not going to die
		name = gene_pillars.437.b

		random_list = {
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 }
			}
			3 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
				gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # This can’t be real
		name = gene_pillars.437.c
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 2 }
		}
		highlight = yes

		random_list = {
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
			3 = {
				gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Peer through the cracks
		name = gene_pillars.437.e
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = ranger }
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 3 }
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 3 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 15 }
	}

	option = { # Set up a snare
		name = gene_pillars.437.f
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = rogue }
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 3 }
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 3 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 15 }
	}

	option = { # Just kill it already
		name = gene_pillars.437.g
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = fighter }
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 3 }
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 3 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 15 }
	}
	
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event
			country_event = {
				id = gene_pillars.438
			}
		}
	}
}

			}
			hidden_effect = {

			}
			gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 511 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = gene_pillar_is_exploring_level_2_pillar
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				gene_pillars_set_up_progress_bar = { events = 14 }
			}
			gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 531 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = gene_pillar_is_exploring_level_3_pillar
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				gene_pillars_set_up_progress_bar = { events = 14 }
			}
			gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 541 }
		}
	}

	# after = { hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }
}

		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.511.b
		if = {
			limit = { culture_group = yenbenmirra }

		}
		else = {
			random = {
				chance = 25
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.511.c
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = ranger }
		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.511.d
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = rogue }
		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 5 }
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.511.e

			culture_is_kanolowele_native_country = yes
		}
		highlight = yes
		add_adm_power = 50
		add_dip_power = 50
		add_mil_power = 50

		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 512 advance = yes }
	}
}

			gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
		else = {

		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.517
	title = gene_pillars.517.t
	desc = gene_pillars.517.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.517.a
		gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		random = {
			chance = 25
			gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.517.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_amount_of_archetype_in_party = { amount = 2 archetype = fighter }
				gene_pillars_has_amount_of_archetype_in_party = { amount = 2 archetype = ranger }
				AND = {
					gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = fighter }
					gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = ranger }
				}
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.517.c
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = rogue }
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = mage }
		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 3 }
		random = {
			chance = 50
			gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
		random = {
			chance = 25
			gene_pillar_injure_random_party_member_effect = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.517.d
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = cleric }
				culture_group = mechanim
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		if = {
			limit = { culture_group = mechanim }
			gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 15 }
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					gene_pillars_add_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
				}
				1 = {
					gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.517.e
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = fighter }
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = ranger }
			}
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = rogue }
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
			}
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = mage }
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = cleric }
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 15 }
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 518 advance = yes }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.518
	title = gene_pillars.518.t
	desc = gene_pillars.518.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.518.a
		gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		add_prestige = 1
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.518.b
		random = {
			chance = 50
			gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.518.c
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 3 }
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.518.d
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_amount_of_archetype_in_party = { amount = 2 archetype = fighter }
		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.518.e
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = fighter }
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = ranger }
			}
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = rogue }
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
			}
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = mage }
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = cleric }
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 3 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 15 }
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 519 advance = yes }
	}
}

#The Acorn Trove
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.519
	title = gene_pillars.519.t
	desc = gene_pillars.519.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.519.a
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.519.b
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 15 }
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.519.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = rogue }
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 25 }
		random = {
			chance = 25
			gene_pillar_injure_random_party_member_effect = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.519.d
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_flamesong_mage_in_party = yes
		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.519.e
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = ranger }
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = rogue }
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
		}
		highlight = yes
		country_event = {
			id = gene_pillars.520
			days = 1
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 521 advance = yes }
	}
}

#The Stash Owner
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.520
	title = gene_pillars.520.t
	desc = gene_pillars.520.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.520.a
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 25 }
		event_target:gene_pillar_exploration_province = {
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = gene_pillars_hinuisquirrel_packbeast
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}
}

#The Ascent
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.521
	title = gene_pillars.521.t
	desc = gene_pillars.521.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.521.a
		event_target:gene_pillar_exploration_province = {
			add_base_tax = 1
			add_base_production = 1
			add_base_manpower = 1
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_province_modifier = gene_pillars_hinuisquirrel_packbeast
				}
				owner = {
					add_prestige = 5
					add_adm_power = 50
					add_dip_power = 50
					add_mil_power = 50
				}
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		gene_pillar_end_expedition_effect = yes
	}
}

### LEVEL 2 Forest Pillar events - The Stem
#Low Functionality
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.531
	title = gene_pillars.531.t
	desc = gene_pillars.531.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.531.a
		gene_pillars_lose_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_loot_effect = { amount = 15 }
			}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 15 }
			}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_add_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.531.b
		random_list = {
			1 = { 
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 } 
			}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 20 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.531.c
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		change_innovativeness = 5
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.531.d
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_flamesong_mage_in_party = yes
		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 20 }
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.531.e
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = rogue }
		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 3 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 532 advance = yes }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.535
	title = gene_pillars.535.t
	desc = gene_pillars.535.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.535.a
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		random = {
			chance = 25
			gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.535.b
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		random = {
			chance = 50
			gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.535.c
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_amount_of_archetype_in_party = { amount = 2 archetype = ranger }
		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 3 }
		random = {
			chance = 10
			gene_pillar_injure_random_party_member_effect = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.535.d
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_stonestory_mage_in_party = yes
			gene_pillars_has_cleric_in_party = yes
		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 15 }
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.535.e
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				culture_group = mechanim
				gene_pillars_has_amount_of_mechanim_country = { amount = 2 }
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 15 }
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 536 advance = yes }
	}
}

	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture

		}

#Verdant Laboratory
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.537
	title = gene_pillars.537.t
	desc = gene_pillars.537.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.537.a
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 5 }
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.537.b
		if = {
			limit = { culture_group = yenbenmirra }
			gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		}
		else = {
			gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			random = {
				chance = 25
				gene_pillars_add_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.537.c
		trigger = {
			event_target:gene_pillar_exploration_province = {
				has_province_modifier = gene_pillars_hinuisquirrel_packbeast
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 20 }
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.537.d
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
		}
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 15 }
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.537.e
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_amount_of_archetype_in_party = { amount = 3 archetype = ranger }
		}
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 3 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 25 }
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 538 advance = yes }
	}
}

			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = fighter }
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = ranger }
			}
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = rogue }
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
			}
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = mage }
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = cleric }
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 15 }
		random = {
			chance = 10
			gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.541.d
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 3 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 5 }
		random = {
			chance = 10
			gene_pillar_injure_random_party_member_effect = yes
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 542 advance = yes }
	}
}

#The Countless Twins
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.542
	title = gene_pillars.542.t
	desc = gene_pillars.542.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.542.a
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 5 }
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.542.b
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.542.c
		trigger = {
			any_owned_province = {
				has_province_modifier = sole_forest
			}
			any_owned_province = {
				has_terrain = forest
				NOT = {
					has_province_modifier = sole_forest
				}
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		random_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				has_terrain = forest
				NOT = {
					has_province_modifier = sole_forest
				}
			}
			add_permanent_province_modifier = {
				name = sole_forest
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.542.d
		trigger = {
			any_owned_province = {
				has_province_modifier = sole_forest
			}
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
		}
		highlight = yes
		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				has_province_modifier = sole_forest
			}
			remove_province_modifier = sole_forest
			add_province_modifier = {
				name = sole_forest_enhanced_growth
				duration = -1
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.542.e
		trigger = {
			culture_group = yenbenmirra
		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		add_prestige = 10
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 543 advance = yes }
	}
}

		add_stability = 1
		add_legitimacy_equivalent = { amount = 10 republican_tradition = 3 }
		event_target:gene_pillar_exploration_province = {
			add_base_tax = 2
			add_base_production = 2
			add_base_manpower = 2
		}
	}

	after = {

			clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_exploration_events_double_speed
		}
		gene_pillar_end_expedition_effect = yes
	}
}

	desc = gene_pillars.611.d
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event
			6950 = { add_province_modifier = { name = gene_pillars_spirit_myow duration = -1 } } # in case he ran off
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.611.a
		random = {
			chance = 50
			gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
	}
	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.611.b
		trigger = { culture_is_harimari = yes }
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 3 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
	}
	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.611.c
		trigger = { 6950 = { has_province_modifier = gene_pillars_spirit_myow } }
		highlight = yes
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_additional_pending_event }
		country_event = { id = gene_pillars.612 }
	}
	after = {
		if = {
			limit = { NOT = { has_country_flag = gene_pillars_additional_pending_event } }
			gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 613 advance = yes }
			hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		}
	}
}

			country_event = { id = gene_pillars.629 }
		}
	}

# Sealed Once More
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.629
	title = gene_pillars.629.t
	desc = gene_pillars.629.d
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}
	is_triggered_only = yes

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }
	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.629.a
		6950 = { remove_province_modifier = gene_pillars_spirit_return_of_tower_master }
		if = {
			limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = gene_pillars_spirit_lock_power value = 4 } }
			gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 25 }
			gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 5 }
			custom_tooltip = gene_pillars_spirit_ending_1
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = gene_pillars_spirit_lock_power value = 3 } }
			gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 20 }
			gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 4 }
			custom_tooltip = gene_pillars_spirit_ending_2
			6950 = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = gene_pillars_spirit_whispers
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = { is_variable_equal = { which = gene_pillars_spirit_lock_power value = 2 } }
			gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 15 }
			gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 3 }
			custom_tooltip = gene_pillars_spirit_ending_3
			6950 = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = gene_pillars_spirit_haunting
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
			gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
			custom_tooltip = gene_pillars_spirit_ending_4
			6950 = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = gene_pillars_spirit_shattered
					duration = -1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	after = {
		gene_pillar_end_expedition_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
	}
}
