	id = gene_pillars.700
	title = gene_pillars.700.t
	desc = gene_pillars.700.d
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	# immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	#Next event
	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.700.a
		
		# gene_pillars_check_extra_hp_at_start = yes

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = gene_pillars_kraken_injure_next_expedition
			}
			gene_pillar_injure_random_party_member_effect = yes
			clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_kraken_injure_next_expedition
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = gene_pillar_is_exploring_level_1_pillar
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				gene_pillars_set_up_progress_bar = { events = 10 }
			}
			gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 711 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = gene_pillar_is_exploring_level_2_pillar
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				gene_pillars_set_up_progress_bar = { events = 12 }
			}
			gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 721 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = gene_pillar_is_exploring_level_3_pillar
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				gene_pillars_set_up_progress_bar = { events = 14 }
			}
			gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 731 }
		}
	}

	# after = { hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }
}

			OR = {

			}
		}

	}

		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_all_mechanim_party_country = yes
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 5 }

		trigger = {

					OR = {

				gene_pillars_has_stonestory_mage_in_party = yes
				gene_pillars_has_artificer_in_party = yes

		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
	}

country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.712
	title = gene_pillars.712.t
	desc = gene_pillars.712.d
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # squeeze tight
		name = gene_pillars.712.a

		random_list = {
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
			}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # get hacking 
		name = gene_pillars.712.b
		
		gene_pillars_lose_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
	}

	option = { # cast fireball
		name = gene_pillars.712.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_wavesong_mage_in_party = yes
				gene_pillars_has_stonescrawl_mage_in_party = yes
				gene_pillars_has_stonestory_mage_in_party = yes
				gene_pillars_has_mage_in_party = yes
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 20 }
		random_list = {
			1 = {
			}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
				gene_pillars_lose_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # like mining
		name = gene_pillars.712.e
		trigger = {
			ROOT = {
				OR = {
					culture_group = kobold
					culture_group = dwarven
					culture_group = goblin
				}
			} 
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 15 }
		add_prestige = 5
	}

	option = { # manipulate the wood
		name = gene_pillars.712.f
		trigger = { 
			ROOT = {
				culture_group = tagaala
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 3 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 5 }
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_kraken_manipulate_wood
			duration = 365
		}
	}

	option = { # is that a challenge
		name = gene_pillars.712.g
		trigger = { 
			gene_pillars_has_flamesong_mage_in_party = yes
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
	}
	
	after = {	
		gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 713 advance = yes }
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
	}
}

		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 5 }

		}

		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 5 }

		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_ranger_in_party = yes
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = rogue }
				gene_pillars_has_soarer_mechanim_in_party = yes
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = cleric }

	after = {

	}
}

	}

		}
		highlight = yes 
		
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 3 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 5 }
	}

	option = { #  reminiscent of a shell

		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = ranger }
		}
		highlight = yes

	option = { #  excellent for repairs

# Kraken Tank
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.724
	title = gene_pillars.724.t
	desc = gene_pillars.724.d
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # Brace for impact
		name = gene_pillars.724.a

		random_list = {
			1 = {}
			2 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
			3 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 }
			}
			4 = {
				gene_pillar_injure_random_party_member_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Ready arms 
		name = gene_pillars.724.b

		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = fighter }
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 2 }
		}
		
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect =  { amount = 20 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					is_or_was_tag = { tag = P24 }
					has_country_modifier = sea_beast_kraken
				}
			}
			gene_pillars_add_loot_effect =  { amount = 20 }
		}
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 }
			}
			1 = {
				gene_pillar_injure_random_party_member_effect  = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Invoke a ward
		name = gene_pillars.724.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = cleric }
					gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 2 }
				}
				is_overall_abjuration_level_1_minimum = yes
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
	}

	option = { # ALL kraken
		name = gene_pillars.724.e
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = mage }
			is_overall_evocation_level_1_minimum = yes
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_injure_entire_party_effect = yes
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_kraken_killed_all_krakens
	}
	
	after = {	
		gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 726 advance = yes }
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
	}
}

		}

		highlight = yes

# Depth-hidden Abominations
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.732
	title = gene_pillars.732.t
	desc = gene_pillars.732.d
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # Bail out the mucus 
		name = gene_pillars.732.a

		if = {
			limit = {
				gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 5 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 4 }
			}
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					gene_pillar_injure_random_party_member_effect = yes
				}
				3 = {}
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					gene_pillar_injure_random_party_member_effect = yes
				}
				1 = {}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Reinforce the bubble (again)
		name = gene_pillars.732.b

		trigger = { 
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = mage }
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
			}
			OR = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						gene_pillars_has_artificer_in_party = yes
						gene_pillars_has_flamesong_mage_in_party = yes
					}
					gene_pillars_has_amount_of_support_class_country = { amount = 1 }
				}
				gene_pillars_has_amount_of_support_class_country = { amount = 2 }
			}
		}
		highlight = yes 
		
		gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
	}

	option = { # anti-magic properties
		name = gene_pillars.732.c

		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
			NOT = { gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = mage } }
		}

		gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 30 }
	}
	
	after = {	
		gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 733 advance = yes }
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
	}
}

#Sandworm Pillar events
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.800
	title = gene_pillars.800.t
	desc = gene_pillars.800.d
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	# immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	#Next event
	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.800.a
		
		# gene_pillars_check_extra_hp_at_start = yes

		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					has_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_hesitant_help
					has_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_enthusiastic_help
				}
			}
			clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_hesitant_help
			clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_enthusiastic_help
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = gene_pillar_is_exploring_level_1_pillar
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				gene_pillars_set_up_progress_bar = { events = 10 }
			}
			gene_pillar_sandworm_pillar_next_event = { specific_event = 811 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = gene_pillar_is_exploring_level_2_pillar
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				gene_pillars_set_up_progress_bar = { events = 12 }
			}
			gene_pillar_sandworm_pillar_next_event = { specific_event = 821 }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = gene_pillar_is_exploring_level_3_pillar
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				gene_pillars_set_up_progress_bar = { events = 14 }
			}
			gene_pillar_sandworm_pillar_next_event = { specific_event = 833 }
		}
	}

	# after = { hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }
}

country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.816
	title = gene_pillars.816.t
	desc = gene_pillars.816.d
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes }

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # members of our team become injured
		name = gene_pillars.816.a

		gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = { # easily avoid this
		name = gene_pillars.816.b
		trigger = {
			ROOT = {
				OR = {
					culture_group = goblin
					culture_group = kobold
					culture_group = halfling
				}
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		random_list = {
			3 = {}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
		}
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
	}

	option = { # A little jury rigging
		name = gene_pillars.816.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = ranger }
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = { # Break a path
		name = gene_pillars.816.e
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_barbarian_in_party = yes
				AND = {
					gene_pillars_has_fighter_in_party = yes
					gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 5 }
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	after = {
		gene_pillar_sandworm_pillar_next_event = { specific_event = 817 }
		gene_pillars_advance_progress_bar = yes
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
	}
}

	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes }

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # Take as many devices
		name = gene_pillars.823.a

		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
	}

	option = { # Try out some
		name = gene_pillars.823.b
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_add_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Get the devices operational
		name = gene_pillars.823.c
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 2 }
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 15 }
	}

	option = { # Use an eye for value
		name = gene_pillars.823.e
		trigger = { 
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = rogue }
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 20 }
	}

	after = {
		gene_pillar_sandworm_pillar_next_event = { specific_event = 824 }
		gene_pillars_advance_progress_bar = yes
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
	}
}

# Tight Twists
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.824
	title = gene_pillars.824.t
	desc = gene_pillars.824.d
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes }

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # We need to back track
		name = gene_pillars.824.a

		gene_pillars_lose_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = { # push through
		name = gene_pillars.824.b

		random_list = {
			1 = {}
			1 = { 
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 }
			}
		}
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 5 }
	}

	option = { # superior pathfinding skills
		name = gene_pillars.824.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = ranger }
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = rogue }
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		random_list = {
			3 = {}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
		}
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
	}

	option = { # This is not that bad
		name = gene_pillars.824.e
		trigger = {
			ROOT = {
				OR = {
					culture_group = dwarven
					culture_group = goblin
					culture_group = kobold
				}
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 15 }
	}

	after = {
		gene_pillar_sandworm_pillar_next_event = { specific_event = 825 }
		gene_pillars_advance_progress_bar = yes
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.827
	title = gene_pillars.827.t
	desc = gene_pillars.827.d
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes }

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # find another way
		name = gene_pillars.827.a

		gene_pillars_lose_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = { #  well placed jumps
		name = gene_pillars.827.b

		random_list = {
			1 = {}
			1 = { 
				gene_pillar_injure_random_party_member_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Fly, you fools!
		name = gene_pillars.827.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_soarer_mechanim_in_party = yes
				culture_group = harpy
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = { # use the grappling hooks
		name = gene_pillars.827.e
		trigger = {
			any_owned_province = {
				trade_goods = wool
				has_manufactory_trigger = yes
			}
			any_owned_province = {
				trade_goods = iron
				has_manufactory_trigger = yes
			}
			ruler_has_personality = industrious_personality
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 3 }
	}

	option = { # shimmy alongside the supports
		name = gene_pillars.827.f
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_rogue_in_party = yes
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 2 }
		}
		highlight = yes

		random_list = {
			3 = {}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_injure_class_effect = { class = rogue_A }
			}
		}
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
	}

	after = {
		gene_pillar_sandworm_pillar_next_event = { specific_event = 828 }
		gene_pillars_advance_progress_bar = yes
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
	}
}

# Catalytic Breach
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.830
	title = gene_pillars.830.t
	desc = gene_pillars.830.d
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes }

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # Ahh, it burns!
		name = gene_pillars.830.a

		random_list = {
			1 = { 
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 } 
			}
			1 = { 
				gene_pillar_injure_random_party_member_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # let’s fill it in with debris
		name = gene_pillars.830.b

		gene_pillars_lose_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		random_list = {
			3 = {}
			1 = { 
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 } 
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # make something to neutralize it
		name = gene_pillars.830.c
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 2 }
		}
		highlight = yes
		
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
		change_innovativeness = 2
	}

	option = { # I got this!
		name = gene_pillars.830.e
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = mage }
			OR = {
				has_reform = mission_of_flamesong
				has_reform = virtues_of_flamesong
				has_reform = grant_noble_flamesong_rights
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		random_list = {
			3 = {}
			1 = { 
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 } 
			}
		}
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_sandworm_landslide_exemplar
			duration = 1825
		}
	}

	after = {
		gene_pillar_sandworm_pillar_next_event = { specific_event = 831 }
		gene_pillars_advance_progress_bar = yes
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
	}
}

		}

		custom_tooltip = gene_pillars_sandworm_benefical_later
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_looked_up_stumbles

		gene_pillar_sandworm_pillar_next_event = { specific_event = 834 }

# Something Is Off
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.834
	title = gene_pillars.834.t
	desc = gene_pillars.834.d
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes }

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # Keep up
		name = gene_pillars.834.a

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				culture_group = mechanim
			}
			set_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_soft_awakening
		}
		else = { 
			set_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_rude_awakening 
		}
	}

	option = { # Break something
		name = gene_pillars.834.b

		gene_pillars_lose_loot_effect = { amount = 5 }
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_rude_awakening
	}

	option = { # I have an idea
		name = gene_pillars.834.c
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 3 }
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_soft_awakening
	}

	option = { # We know who they are
		name = gene_pillars.834.e
		trigger = { 
			has_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_looked_up_stumbles
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 3 }
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_soft_awakening
	}

	after = {
		
		gene_pillar_sandworm_pillar_next_event = { specific_event = 835 }
		gene_pillars_advance_progress_bar = yes
		hidden_effect = { 
			clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_looked_up_stumbles
			clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event 
		}
	}
}

# A Breakthrough
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.835
	title = gene_pillars.835.t
	desc = gene_pillars.835.d
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes }

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # We have a plan
		name = gene_pillars.835.a

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_soft_awakening }
			gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
			random_list = {
				1 = { 
					set_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_hesitant_help 
					custom_tooltip = gene_pillars_sandworm_hesitant_tt
				}
				3 = { 
					set_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_enthusiastic_help 
					custom_tooltip = gene_pillars_sandworm_enthusiastic_tt
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				1 = { 
					set_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_hesitant_help 
					custom_tooltip = gene_pillars_sandworm_hesitant_tt
				}
				1 = { 
					set_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_enthusiastic_help
					custom_tooltip = gene_pillars_sandworm_enthusiastic_tt
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # We are going to insist
		name = gene_pillars.835.b

		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_hesitant_help
		custom_tooltip = gene_pillars_sandworm_hesitant_tt
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 15 }
	}

	option = { # We can set you free
		name = gene_pillars.835.c
		trigger = {
			culture_group = mechanim
		}
		highlight = yes

		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_enthusiastic_help
		custom_tooltip = gene_pillars_sandworm_enthusiastic_tt
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_modifier = mechanim_military
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = gene_pillars_sandworm_repair_expertise
				duration = 1825
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # we can make it out of here.
		name = gene_pillars.835.e
		trigger = {
			ruler_has_personality = kind_hearted_personality
		}
		highlight = yes
		
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_enthusiastic_help
		custom_tooltip = gene_pillars_sandworm_enthusiastic_tt
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 3 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
	}

	after = {
		gene_pillar_sandworm_pillar_next_event = { specific_event = 836 }
		gene_pillars_advance_progress_bar = yes
		hidden_effect = { 
			clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_soft_awakening
			clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_rude_awakening
			clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event 
		}
	}
}

# Savannah River
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.836
	title = gene_pillars.836.t
	desc = gene_pillars.836.d
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes }

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # We can carry it across
		name = gene_pillars.836.a

		random_list = {
			3 = {}
			1 = { 
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 } 
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_hesitant_help }
			random_list = {
				1 = {}
				1 = { 
					gene_pillars_lose_xp_effect = { amount = 1 } 
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # construct a makeshift raft.
		name = gene_pillars.836.b

		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_enthusiastic_help }
			random_list = {
				1 = {}
				1 = { 
					gene_pillars_lose_xp_effect = { amount = 2 } 
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				1 = {}
				3 = {
					gene_pillars_lose_xp_effect = { amount = 2 } 
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # We can levitate it
		name = gene_pillars.836.c
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = mage }
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 2 }
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_hesitant_help }
			random_list = {
				1 = {}
				1 = { 
					set_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_enthusiastic_help 
					clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_hesitant_help 
					custom_tooltip = gene_pillars_sandworm_enthusiastic_tt
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # swim across
		name = gene_pillars.836.e
		trigger = {
			culture_group = lizardfolk
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_hesitant_help }
			random_list = {
				3 = {}
				1 = { 
					set_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_enthusiastic_help 
					clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_hesitant_help 
					custom_tooltip = gene_pillars_sandworm_enthusiastic_tt
				}
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		gene_pillar_sandworm_pillar_next_event = { specific_event = 837 }
		gene_pillars_advance_progress_bar = yes
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
	}
}

# Parasite Ambush!
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.837
	title = gene_pillars.837.t
	desc = gene_pillars.837.d
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes }

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # We got you!
		name = gene_pillars.837.a

		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_enthusiastic_help }
			random_list = { 
				1 = {} 
				1 = { 
					gene_pillar_injure_random_party_member_effect = yes 
				} 
			}
			random_list = { 
				3 = {} 
				1 = { 
					gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 } 
				} 
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = { 
				1 = {} 
				3 = { 
					gene_pillar_injure_random_party_member_effect = yes
				} 
			}
			random_list = { 
				1 = {} 
				1 = { 
					gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 } 
				} 
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Let me handle this
		name = gene_pillars.837.b
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_fighter_in_party = yes
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 2 }
			OR = {
				culture_group = troll
				culture_group = ogre
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		random_list = {
			3 = {}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_injure_class_effect = { class = fighter_A }
			}
		}
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 5 }
	}

	option = { # Beast begone!

		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = cleric }
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 2 }
		}
		highlight = yes

		random_list = { 
			3 = {} 
			1 = { 
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 } 
			} 
		}
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 3 }
	}

	option = { # Swing out
		name = gene_pillars.837.e
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_ranger_in_party = yes
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 3 }
		}
		highlight = yes

		random_list = {
			3 = {}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_injure_class_effect = { class = ranger_A }
			 }
		}
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 15 }
	}

	after = {
		gene_pillar_sandworm_pillar_next_event = { specific_event = 838 }
		gene_pillars_advance_progress_bar = yes
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.838
	title = gene_pillars.838.t
	desc = gene_pillars.838.d

		}
		else = {

				1 = {} 
				1 = {

				} 
			}
			random_list = { 
				1 = {} 
				1 = {

				}

					clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_hesitant_help
					custom_tooltip = gene_pillars_sandworm_enthusiastic_tt
				} 
			}
		}
		else = {
			gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = { #  magical and divine

		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = cleric }
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = mage }
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 2 }
		}
		highlight = yes

		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_enthusiastic_help }
			random_list = { 
				3 = {} 
				1 = { 
					gene_pillars_lose_loot_effect = { amount = 5 }
				} 
			}
		}
		else = { 
			random_list = { 
				3 = {} 
				1 = { 
					set_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_enthusiastic_help
					clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_hesitant_help
					custom_tooltip = gene_pillars_sandworm_enthusiastic_tt
				} 
			}
			random_list = { 
				1 = {} 
				1 = { 
					gene_pillars_lose_loot_effect = { amount = 5 }
				} 
			} 
		}
	}

	after = {

	}

	option = { # We have a sense for it.

			}

				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 }
			}

		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 3 }
		}

# The Inner Chambers
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.842
	title = gene_pillars.842.t
	desc = gene_pillars.842.d
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes }

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # Go, go, go
		name = gene_pillars.842.a
		trigger = { 
			hidden_trigger = {
				has_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_rushed_inner_chambers
			}
		}

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		random = {
			chance = 25
			gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
		random = {
			chance = 25
			gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
		random = {
			chance = 25
			gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
		clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_rushed_inner_chambers
	}

	option = { # lead us through.
		name = gene_pillars.842.b
		trigger = { 
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = { 
					has_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_rushed_inner_chambers 
				}
			}
		}

		if = {
			limit = { has_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_enthusiastic_help }
			random = {
				chance = 25
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
		}
		else = { 
			random = {
				chance = 50
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # We can seek out a safe path.
		name = gene_pillars.842.c
		trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = { 
					has_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_rushed_inner_chambers 
				}
			}
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = ranger }
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = rogue }
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 2 }
		}

		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
	}

	option = { # Channel magic to overload part of the grid.
		name = gene_pillars.842.e
		trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = { 
					has_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_rushed_inner_chambers 
				}
			}
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = mage }
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 3 }
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
	}

	option = { # We can get beneath the floor, and move under it.
		name = gene_pillars.842.f
		trigger = {
			hidden_trigger = {
				NOT = { 
					has_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_rushed_inner_chambers 
				}
			}
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = rogue }
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 3 }
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 15 }
	}

	after = {

# The Mechanical Great Worm
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.843
	title = gene_pillars.843.t
	desc = gene_pillars.843.d
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes }

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # final stand
		name = gene_pillars.843.a

		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						gene_pillars_has_any_frontliner_class_country = yes
						gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 2 }
					}
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						gene_pillars_has_amount_of_frontliner_class_country = { amount = 2 }
						gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 2 }
					}
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = cleric }
						gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 3 }
					}
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					AND = {
						gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
						gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 3 }
					}
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				NOT = {
					has_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_enthusiastic_help
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
		}
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
	}

	option = { # blow it up
		name = gene_pillars.843.b
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = mage }
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = rogue }
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 3 }
			ruler_has_personality = intricate_web_weaver_personality
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 20 }
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 3 }
		add_prestige = 15
	}

	after = {
		gene_pillar_sandworm_pillar_next_event = { specific_event = 844 }
		gene_pillars_advance_progress_bar = yes
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
	}
}

# A Small Solace
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.844
	title = gene_pillars.844.t
	desc = gene_pillars.844.d
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes }

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # plan ahead
		name = gene_pillars.844.a

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = { # enjoy the spoils of victory
		name = gene_pillars.844.b

		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
	}

	option = { # Split up the remaining tasks
		name = gene_pillars.844.c
		
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = fighter }
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = rogue }
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = cleric }
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = mage }
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
	}

	option = { # A soothing touch
		name = gene_pillars.844.e
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = cleric }
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 2 }
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		add_estate_loyalty = {
			estate = estate_church
			loyalty = 10
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				ruler_has_personality = zealot_personality
			}
			gene_pillars_add_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
	}

	after = {
		gene_pillar_sandworm_pillar_next_event = { specific_event = 845 }
		gene_pillars_advance_progress_bar = yes
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
	}
}

# The Final Component
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.845
	title = gene_pillars.845.t
	desc = gene_pillars.845.d
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes }

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # Give it a try
		name = gene_pillars.845.a

		random_list = { 
			1 = {}
			1 = { 
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 3 } 
			} 
		}
	}

	option = { # try to sneak in.
		name = gene_pillars.845.b
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = rogue }
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 3 }
		}
		highlight = yes

		random_list = { 
			3 = {}
			1 = { 
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 } 
			} 
		}
	}

	option = { # Redirect some gas
		name = gene_pillars.845.c
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = mage }
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 3 }
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 25 }
	}

	option = { # make a replacement
		name = gene_pillars.845.e
		trigger = {
			has_country_flag = gene_pillars_sandworm_enthusiastic_help
			gene_pillars_has_amount_of_archetype_in_party = { amount = 2 archetype = artificer }
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 3 }
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
	}

	after = {
		gene_pillar_sandworm_pillar_next_event = { specific_event = 846 }
		gene_pillars_advance_progress_bar = yes
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
	}
}

# Forcing the lower gate
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.911
	title = gene_pillars.911.t
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_barbarian_in_party = yes
				gene_pillars_has_warrior_mechanim_in_party = yes
			}
		}
		desc = gene_pillars.911.desc.barbarian_warrior_mechanim
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			always = yes
		}
		desc = gene_pillars.911.desc
	}
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # Use brute force
		name = gene_pillars.911.a
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_warrior_mechanim_in_party = yes
				gene_pillars_has_barbarian_in_party = yes
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		add_yearly_manpower = -0.5
		add_adm_power = -5
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_dragon_shock_damage
			duration = 730 # 2 years
		}
	}

	option = { # Use some acid
		name = gene_pillars.911.b

		add_yearly_manpower = -0.5
		add_mil_power = -5
		add_adm_power = -5
		add_years_of_income = -0.1
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = { # Use acid and replace it
		name = gene_pillars.911.c
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_artificer_in_party = yes
		}
		highlight = yes

		add_yearly_manpower = -0.5
		add_mil_power = -5
		add_adm_power = -5
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
	}
	
	after = {	
		gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 912 advance = yes }
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.915
	title = gene_pillars.915.t
	desc = gene_pillars.915.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture

	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.915.a
		
		add_prestige = -15
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.915.b
		trigger = {
			government = republic
			has_government_attribute = is_merchant_republic
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
		event_target:gene_pillar_exploration_province = {
			add_base_tax = 1
			add_base_manpower = -1
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.915.c
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_mage_in_party = yes
			has_mana = { amount = 10 }
		}
		highlight = yes
		
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		change_mana = { amount = -10 }
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.915.d
		trigger = {
			ruler_has_personality = greedy_personality
		}
		highlight = yes

		add_years_of_income = 0.5
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 15 }
		add_prestige = -10
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.915.e
		trigger = {
			ruler_has_personality = scholar_personality
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_dragon_tech_cost_5
			duration = 730 # 2 years
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.915.f
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				culture_is_harpy = yes
				gene_pillars_has_soarer_mechanim_in_party = yes
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		add_prestige = 10
	}
	
	after = {
		hidden_effect = {
			clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event
			# Extra ending event for this chain
			country_event = {
				id = gene_pillars.916
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.924
	title = gene_pillars.924.t
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			primary_culture_insyaa_kobold = yes
		}
		desc = gene_pillars.924.desc.insyaa_kobold
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			is_cannorian_kobold_primary_culture = yes
		}
		desc = gene_pillars.924.desc.cannor_kobold
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			always = yes
		}
		desc = gene_pillars.924.desc.non_kobold
	}
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.924.a
		trigger = {
			culture_is_kobold = no
		}

		every_owned_province = {
			limit = {
				fast_has_pop_of_race = { race = kobold }
			}
			add_unrest = 2
		}
		add_dip_power = 5
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.924.b
		trigger = {
			culture_is_kobold = no
			NOT = {
				ruler_has_personality = kind_personality
				high_tolerance_kobold_race_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_dragon_tech_cost_10
			duration = 1825 # 5 years
		}
		generic_decrease_of_racial_tolerance_effect = { race = kobold largest = yes }
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.924.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = { culture_is_kobold = yes }
			ruler_has_personality = kind_personality
		}

		}

	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.924.d
		trigger = {
			primary_culture_insyaa_kobold = yes
		}
		
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_dragon_unrest_2
			duration = 1825 # 5 years
		}
		random = {
			chance = 20
			add_stability = -1
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.924.e
		trigger = {
			culture_is_kobold = yes
			ruler_has_personality = kind_personality
		}
		highlight = yes

		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_dragon_unrest_minus_2
			duration = 1825 # 5 years
		}
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.924.f
		trigger = {
			is_cannorian_kobold_primary_culture = yes
		}
		highlight = yes

		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_dragon_unrest_2
			duration = 1825 # 5 years
		}
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }

	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture

	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.931.a
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_mage_in_party = yes
			is_estate_enchantment_level_3 = yes
			has_mana = { amount = 10 }
		}
		highlight = yes

		add_mil_power = 30
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		change_mana = { amount = -10 }
		add_estate_influence_modifier = {
			estate = estate_mages
			desc = EST_GENE_PILLAR_MAGE_UNPICK_VAULT_SPELL
			influence = 5
			duration = 1825 # 5 years
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.931.b
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_mage_in_party = yes
			hidden_trigger = { NOT = { is_estate_enchantment_level_3 = yes } }
			has_mana = { amount = 50 }
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		change_mana = { amount = -50 }
		add_estate_influence_modifier = {
			estate = estate_mages
			desc = EST_GENE_PILLAR_MAGE_UNPICK_VAULT_SPELL
			influence = 5
			duration = 1825 # 5 years
		}
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_exploration_next_event_small_delay
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.931.c
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_artificer_in_party = yes
			tier_3_artificer_estate = yes
		}
		highlight = yes

		add_adm_power = 10
		add_dip_power = 10
		add_mil_power = 10
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		add_years_of_income = -0.25
		add_estate_influence_modifier = {
			estate = estate_artificers
			desc = EST_GENE_PILLAR_ARTIFICER_KEY
			influence = 5
			duration = 1825 # 5 years
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.931.d
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_artificer_in_party = yes
			hidden_trigger = { NOT = { tier_3_artificer_estate = yes } }
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		add_years_of_income = -0.5
		add_estate_influence_modifier = {
			estate = estate_artificers
			desc = EST_GENE_PILLAR_ARTIFICER_KEY
			influence = 5
			duration = 1825 # 5 years
		}
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_exploration_next_event_small_delay
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.931.e
		trigger = {
			culture_is_elven = yes
			has_estate = estate_mages
			has_mana = { amount = 50 }
		}
		highlight = yes

		add_mil_power = 10
		change_mana = { amount = -50 }
		add_estate_influence_modifier = {
			estate = estate_mages
			desc = EST_GENE_PILLAR_MAGE_ELVES
			influence = 5
			duration = 1825 # 5 years
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.931.f
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_rogue_in_party = yes
		}
		highlight = yes

		add_adm_power = -10
		add_dip_power = -10
		add_mil_power = -10
		add_years_of_income = -0.25
		add_estate_loyalty_modifier = {
			estate = estate_nobles
			desc = EST_GENE_PILLAR_NOBLES_ROGUE
			loyalty = -10
			duration = 1825 # 5 years
		}
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_exploration_next_event_small_delay
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.931.g
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_fighter_in_party = yes
				culture_is_ogre = yes
				culture_is_troll = yes
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		add_mil_power = -25
		add_years_of_income = -0.25
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.931.h
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					has_advisor_of_type_and_level = { type = adm level = 3 }
					has_advisor_of_type_and_level = { type = dip level = 3 }
					has_advisor_of_type_and_level = { type = mil level = 3 }
				}
				ruler_has_personality = scholar_personality
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		add_adm_power = -25
		add_dip_power = -25
		add_mil_power = -25
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_exploration_next_event_medium_delay
	}

	option = {

		add_dip_power = -25
		add_mil_power = -25
		add_years_of_income = -0.75
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_exploration_next_event_large_delay
	}
	
	after = {
		gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 932 advance = yes }
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
	}

# Inactive precursor power core
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.932
	title = gene_pillars.932.t
	desc = gene_pillars.932.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # The core keeps running
		name = gene_pillars.932.a
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_dragon_power_core_activated_province = yes
		}
		highlight = yes

		add_prestige = 10
	}

	option = { # Nothing is left for us
		name = gene_pillars.932.b
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_dragon_power_core_removed_province = yes
		}
		highlight = yes

		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_dragon_morale_malus
			duration = 730 # 2 years
		}
	}

	option = { # Maybe we can get it going
		name = gene_pillars.932.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				gene_pillars_dragon_power_core_activated_province = yes
				gene_pillars_dragon_power_core_removed_province = yes
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				hidden_effect = { 6386 = { set_province_flag = gene_pillar_dragon_power_core_activated } }
				custom_tooltip = gene_pillar_dragon_power_core_activate_success_tt
			}
			8 = {}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 }
				hidden_effect = { 6386 = { set_province_flag = gene_pillar_dragon_damestear_removed } }
				custom_tooltip = gene_pillar_dragon_power_core_remove_tt
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Try replacing the power source
		name = gene_pillars.932.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				gene_pillars_dragon_power_core_activated_province = yes
				gene_pillars_dragon_power_core_removed_province = yes
			}
			damestear = 1
			NOT = { precursor_relics = 1 }
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		add_years_of_income = -0.25
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				hidden_effect = { 6386 = { set_province_flag = gene_pillar_dragon_power_core_activated } }
				custom_tooltip = gene_pillar_dragon_power_core_activate_success_tt
			}
			1 = {}
		}
	}

	option = { # We have seen things like this
		name = gene_pillars.932.e
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				gene_pillars_dragon_power_core_activated_province = yes
				gene_pillars_dragon_power_core_removed_province = yes
			}
			precursor_relics = 1
			NOT = { damestear = 1 }
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		add_years_of_income = -0.25
		random_list = {
			33 = {
				hidden_effect = { 6386 = { set_province_flag = gene_pillar_dragon_power_core_activated } }
				custom_tooltip = gene_pillar_dragon_power_core_activate_success_tt
			}
			66 = {}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
				hidden_effect = { 6386 = { set_province_flag = gene_pillar_dragon_damestear_removed } }
				custom_tooltip = gene_pillar_dragon_power_core_remove_tt
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # With an update to the power...
		name = gene_pillars.932.f
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				gene_pillars_dragon_power_core_activated_province = yes
				gene_pillars_dragon_power_core_removed_province = yes
			}
			precursor_relics = 1
			damestear = 1
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		add_years_of_income = -0.5
		hidden_effect = { 6386 = { set_province_flag = gene_pillar_dragon_power_core_activated } }
		custom_tooltip = gene_pillar_dragon_power_core_activate_success_tt
	}

	option = { # Contain and manipulate
		name = gene_pillars.932.g
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				gene_pillars_dragon_power_core_activated_province = yes
				gene_pillars_dragon_power_core_removed_province = yes
			}
			gene_pillars_has_mage_in_party = yes
			is_estate_enchantment_level_1_minimum = yes
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		add_years_of_income = -0.5
		hidden_effect = { 6386 = { set_province_flag = gene_pillar_dragon_power_core_activated } }
		custom_tooltip = gene_pillar_dragon_power_core_activate_success_tt
	}

	option = { # This should go like this...
		name = gene_pillars.932.h
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				gene_pillars_dragon_power_core_activated_province = yes
				gene_pillars_dragon_power_core_removed_province = yes
			}
			gene_pillars_has_artificer_in_party = yes
			tier_2_artificer_estate = yes
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		add_years_of_income = -0.5
		hidden_effect = { 6386 = { set_province_flag = gene_pillar_dragon_power_core_activated } }
		custom_tooltip = gene_pillar_dragon_power_core_activate_success_tt
	}

	option = { # Just like a disarming a trap
		name = gene_pillars.932.i

		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				gene_pillars_dragon_power_core_activated_province = yes
				gene_pillars_dragon_power_core_removed_province = yes
			}
			gene_pillars_has_rogue_in_party = yes
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		random = {
			chance = 50
			hidden_effect = { 6386 = { set_province_flag = gene_pillar_dragon_power_core_activated } }
			custom_tooltip = gene_pillar_dragon_power_core_activate_success_tt
		}
	}

	option = { # There is damestear here...
		name = gene_pillars.932.j

		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				gene_pillars_dragon_power_core_activated_province = yes

			}
		}
		highlight = yes

	after = {

# Draconic suppression matrix
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.933
	title = gene_pillars.933.t
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_kobold_in_party = yes
			gene_pillars_dragon_power_core_activated_province = yes
		}
		desc = gene_pillars.933.desc.kobold_active_power
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_dragon_power_core_activated_province = yes
		}
		desc = gene_pillars.933.desc.active_power
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			always = yes
		}
		desc = gene_pillars.933.desc.other
	}
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		if = { ### placeholder tooltip, or extra event text?
			limit = {
				gene_pillars_dragon_power_core_activated_province = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = {
					culture_is_kobold = yes
				}
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 }
				set_country_flag = gene_pillar_dragon_kobold_suppression # 50% -1 HP on subsequent encounters
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						high_tolerance_kobold_race_trigger = yes
						medium_tolerance_kobold_race_trigger = yes
					}
				}
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
				set_country_flag = gene_pillar_dragon_kobold_suppression # 50% -1 HP on subsequent encounters
			}
			gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		}
	}

	option = { # destroy it
		name = gene_pillars.933.a
		
		generic_increase_of_racial_tolerance_effect = { race = kobold large = yes }
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					high_tolerance_kobold_race_trigger = yes
					culture_is_kobold = yes
				}
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = gene_pillars_dragon_unrest_minus_2
				duration = 9125 # 25 years
			}
		}
		add_dip_power = 15
		event_target:gene_pillar_exploration_province = {
			set_province_flag = gene_pillars_dragon_suppression_disabled
		}
	}

	option = { # turn it off
		name = gene_pillars.933.b

		if = {
			limit = {
				gene_pillars_dragon_power_core_activated_province = yes
			}
			hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_draconic_suppress_deactivated }
		}
		add_adm_power = 15
		event_target:gene_pillar_exploration_province = {
			set_province_flag = gene_pillars_dragon_suppression_disabled
		}
	}

	option = { # We can use this
		name = gene_pillars.933.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				culture_is_kobold = yes
				high_tolerance_kobold_race_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		generic_decrease_of_racial_tolerance_effect = { race = kobold large = yes }
		custom_tooltip = gene_pillar_dragon_kobold_suppress_tt
		hidden_effect = {
			every_owned_province = {
				limit = {
					fast_has_pop_of_race = { race = kobold }
				}
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = gene_pillars_dragon_kobold_unrest_minus_2
					duration = 9125 # 25 years
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				gene_pillars_dragon_power_core_activated_province = yes
			}
			hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_draconic_suppress_deactivated }
		}
	}

	option = { # Can we adapt this to suppress our people?
		name = gene_pillars.933.d
		trigger = {
			ruler_has_personality = cruel_personality
			has_mana = { amount = 25 }
		}
		highlight = yes

		add_dip_power = -25
		change_mana = { amount = -25 }
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_dragon_unrest_minus_2
			duration = 5475 # 15 years
		}
	}

	option = { # Can we learn anything?
		name = gene_pillars.933.e
		trigger = {
			
		}
		highlight = yes

		add_adm_power = 10
		add_dip_power = 10
		add_mil_power = 10
	}

	option = { # It would make a fine trophy
		name = gene_pillars.933.f
		trigger = {
			
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 5 }
			hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_draconic_suppress_deactivated }
	}
	
	after = {
		gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 934 advance = yes }
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
	}
}

# Anatomical study
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.934
	title = gene_pillars.934.t
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			primary_culture_insyaa_kobold = yes
		}
		desc = gene_pillars.934.desc.insyaan_kobold
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			is_cannorian_kobold_primary_culture = yes
		}
		desc = gene_pillars.934.desc.cannor_kobold
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			any_owned_province = {
				NOT = { continent = oceania }
			}
		}
		desc = gene_pillars.934.desc.knows_dragons
	}
	desc = {
		trigger = {
			always = yes
		}
		desc = gene_pillars.934.desc.other
	}
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = gene_pillar_dragon_kobold_suppression
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # How could anyone do this?
		name = gene_pillars.934.a

		trigger = {
			primary_culture_insyaa_kobold = yes
		}
		highlight = yes
		
		random = {
			chance = 50
			add_stability = -1
		}
		add_prestige = -15
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
	}

	option = { # Can we learn anything from this horror?
		name = gene_pillars.934.b

		trigger = {
			primary_culture_insyaa_kobold = yes
			ruler_has_personality = scholar_personality
		}
		highlight = yes

		add_stability = -1
		add_prestige = -25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_dragon_tech_cost_10
			duration = 1825 # 5 years
		}
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
	}

	option = { # A sad day for kobolds
		name = gene_pillars.934.c

		trigger = {
			is_cannorian_kobold_primary_culture = yes
		}
		highlight = yes

		random = {
			chance = 50
			add_stability = -1
		}
		add_prestige = -25
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		unlock_kobold_dragon_cult_for_colour_slot_upgrade = {
			COLOUR = black
			SLOT = 3
			UPGRADE = base
		}
	}

	option = { # Can we learn anything from this horror? (non kobold)
		name = gene_pillars.934.d
		trigger = {
			primary_culture_insyaa_kobold = no
			NOT = { ruler_has_personality = scholar_personality }
		}
		highlight = yes

		add_dip_power = -15
		add_prestige = -25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_dragon_tech_cost_10
			duration = 1825 # 5 years
		}
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
	}

	option = { # Can we learn anything from this horror? (non kobold, scholar)
		name = gene_pillars.934.e
		trigger = {
			primary_culture_insyaa_kobold = no
			ruler_has_personality = scholar_personality
		}
		highlight = yes

		add_prestige = -25
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_dragon_tech_cost_10
			duration = 1825 # 5 years
		}
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
	}
	
	after = {
		gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 935 advance = yes }
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
	}
}

# Precursor library
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.935
	title = gene_pillars.935.t
	desc = gene_pillars.935.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		# These damage effects will need to be explained in the event loc
		# Default is 50/50 for -1/-2 hp, but a couple of ways to make it -1/0 hp
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
			1 = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						OR = {
							AND = {
								gene_pillars_has_artificer_in_party = yes
								tier_3_artificer_estate = yes
							}
							AND = {
								gene_pillars_has_mage_in_party = yes
								is_estate_enchantment_level_3 = yes
							}
						}
					}
					gene_pillars_add_hp_effect = { amount = 0 }
				}
				else = {
					gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = gene_pillar_dragon_kobold_suppression
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Draconic Genie Magic: A Primer
		name = gene_pillars.935.a
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_cannorian_kobold_primary_culture = yes
				is_in_artificery_mode = yes
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = gene_pillars_dragon_artifice_cap_20
				duration = -1
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_estate_enchantment_level_3 = yes
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = gene_pillars_dragon_magic_xp_25
				duration = 3650 # 10 yaers
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_estate_enchantment_level_1_minimum = yes
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = gene_pillar_dragon_enchantment_xp
				duration = 3650 # 10 yaers
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_estate = estate_mages
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = gene_pillars_dragon_magic_xp_10
				duration = 3650 # 10 yaers
			}
		}
		else = {
			add_adm_power = 10
			add_dip_power = 10
			add_mil_power = 10
		}

	}

	option = { # Spirits: the future of clean power
		name = gene_pillars.935.b

		if = {
			limit = {
				tier_3_artificer_estate = yes
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = gene_pillars_dragon_artifice_cap_15
				duration = -1
			}
			add_adm_power = 10
			add_dip_power = 10
			add_mil_power = 10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				has_estate = estate_artificers
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = gene_pillars_dragon_artifice_cap_10
				duration = -1
			}
			add_adm_power = 10
			add_dip_power = 10
			add_mil_power = 10
		}
		else = {
			add_adm_power = 10
			add_dip_power = 10
			add_mil_power = 10
		}
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_dragon_book_spirits_chosen
	}

	option = { # On the nature of kobolds
		name = gene_pillars.935.c

		if = {
			limit = {
				primary_culture_insyaa_kobold = yes
			}
			custom_tooltip = every_province_kobold_majority_tt
			tooltip = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = gene_pillars_kobold_productivity
					duration = 3650 # 10 years
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						has_kobold_majority_trigger = yes
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = gene_pillars_kobold_productivity
						duration = 3650 # 10 years
					}
				}
			}
			add_adm_power = 10
			add_dip_power = 10
			add_mil_power = 10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_cannorian_kobold_primary_culture = yes
			}
			add_church_power = 200
			add_adm_power = 10
			add_dip_power = 10
			add_mil_power = 10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				high_tolerance_kobold_race_trigger = yes
			}
			custom_tooltip = every_province_kobold_majority_tt
			tooltip = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = gene_pillars_dragon_kobold_unrest_minus_2
					duration = 3650 # 10 years
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						has_kobold_majority_trigger = yes
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = gene_pillars_dragon_kobold_unrest_minus_2
						duration = 3650 # 10 years
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				medium_tolerance_kobold_race_trigger = yes
			}
			largest_increase_of_kobold_tolerance_effect = yes
			add_adm_power = 10
			add_dip_power = 10
			add_mil_power = 10
		}
		else = {
			add_adm_power = 10
			add_dip_power = 10
			add_mil_power = 10
		}
	}

	option = { # Worlds beyond worlds
		name = gene_pillars.935.d

		if = {
			limit = {
				culture_is_lizardfolk = yes
			}
			custom_tooltip = every_province_lizardfolk_majority_tt
			tooltip = {
				add_province_modifier = {
					name = gene_pillars_dragon_kobold_unrest_minus_2
					duration = 3650 # 10 years
				}
			}
			hidden_effect = {
				every_owned_province = {
					limit = {
						has_lizardfolk_majority_trigger = yes
					}
					add_province_modifier = {
						name = gene_pillars_dragon_kobold_unrest_minus_2
						duration = 3650 # 10 years
					}
				}
			}
			add_country_modifier = {
				name = gene_pillars_dragon_morale_bonus_10
				duration = 3650 # 10 years
			}
			add_adm_power = 10
			add_dip_power = 10
			add_mil_power = 10
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				tag = I03 # Dur-Vazhatun
			}
			vazhatun_add_scaling_knowledge = { AMOUNT = 30 }
			add_adm_power = 25
			add_dip_power = 25
			add_mil_power = 25
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				culture_is_elven = yes
			}
			add_prestige = 25
			add_adm_power = 10
			add_dip_power = 10
			add_mil_power = 10
		}
		else = {
			add_adm_power = 10
			add_dip_power = 10
			add_mil_power = 10
		}
	}
	
	after = {
		gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 936 advance = yes }
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
	}
}

# The Final Seal
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.936
	title = gene_pillars.936.t
	desc = gene_pillars.936.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_country_flag = gene_pillar_dragon_kobold_suppression
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Strong mage shield
		name = gene_pillars.936.a

		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_mage_in_party = yes
			is_estate_abjuration_level_3 = yes
		}
		highlight = yes
		
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 5 }
	}

	option = { # Decent mage shield
		name = gene_pillars.936.b

		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_mage_in_party = yes
			is_estate_abjuration_level_1_minimum = yes
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 }
			}
		}
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 5 }
	}

	option = { # Use small gizmos as shields
		name = gene_pillars.936.c

		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_artificer_in_party = yes
			tier_3_artificer_estate = yes
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 5 }
	}

	option = { # Trying to use small gizmos
		name = gene_pillars.936.d
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_artificer_in_party = yes
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 }
			}
		}
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 5 }
	}

	option = { # It's always traps
		name = gene_pillars.936.e
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 2 }
			gene_pillars_has_rogue_in_party = yes
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 }
			}
		}
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
	}

	option = { # Provide cover
		name = gene_pillars.936.f
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_fighter_in_party = yes
				culture_is_ogre = yes
				culture_is_troll = yes
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 }
			}
		}
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 5 }
	}

	option = { # That was painful
		name = gene_pillars.936.g
		
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		random_list = {
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 }
			}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 3 }
			}
		}
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 5 }
	}
	
	after = {
		gene_pillar_generic_then_specific_event = { specific_event = 937 advance = yes }
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
	}
}

country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.937
	title = gene_pillars.937.t
	desc = gene_pillars.937.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # Best ending
		name = gene_pillars.937.a
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_dragon_power_core_activated_province = yes
			gene_pillars_dragon_suppression_matrix_disabled_province = yes
			has_country_flag = gene_pillars_dragon_book_spirits_chosen
		}
		highlight = yes

		# gain a cool advisor
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_estate = estate_mages
			}
			add_country_modifier = { name = gene_pillars_dragon_court_mage_homunculus duration = -1 }
		}
		else = {
			add_country_modifier = { name = philosopher_homunculus duration = -1 }
		}
	}

	option = { # Missing the book
		name = gene_pillars.937.b
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_dragon_power_core_activated_province = yes
			gene_pillars_dragon_suppression_matrix_disabled_province = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = gene_pillars_dragon_book_spirits_chosen }
		}
		highlight = yes

		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_dragon_apc
			duration = 3650 # 10 years
		}
	}

	option = { # Suppression matrix still on

			gene_pillars_dragon_suppression_matrix_disabled_province = no

		}
		highlight = yes

		add_province_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_dragon_government

		}
	}

	option = { # Core repair only

		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_dragon_power_core_activated_province = yes
			gene_pillars_dragon_suppression_matrix_disabled_province = no
			NOT = { has_country_flag = gene_pillars_dragon_book_spirits_chosen }
		}
		highlight = yes

		add_adm_power = 50
		add_dip_power = 50
		add_mil_power = 50
	}

	option = { # Suppress matrix and book
		name = gene_pillars.937.e
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_dragon_power_core_activated_province = no
			gene_pillars_dragon_suppression_matrix_disabled_province = yes
			has_country_flag = gene_pillars_dragon_book_spirits_chosen
		}
		highlight = yes

		add_adm_power = 50
		add_dip_power = 50
		add_mil_power = 50
	}

	option = { # Primary elves
		name = gene_pillars.937.f
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_dragon_power_core_activated_province = no
			gene_pillars_dragon_suppression_matrix_disabled_province = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = gene_pillars_dragon_book_spirits_chosen }
			culture_is_elven = yes
		}
		highlight = yes

		random_list = {
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Matrix disabled only
		name = gene_pillars.937.g
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_dragon_power_core_activated_province = no
			gene_pillars_dragon_suppression_matrix_disabled_province = yes
			NOT = { has_country_flag = gene_pillars_dragon_book_spirits_chosen }
		}
		highlight = yes

		random_list = {
			1 = {
				add_adm_power = 25
				add_dip_power = 25
				add_mil_power = 25
			}
			1 = {
				add_adm_power = 50
				add_dip_power = 50
				add_mil_power = 50
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Book chosen only
		name = gene_pillars.937.h
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_dragon_power_core_activated_province = no
			gene_pillars_dragon_suppression_matrix_disabled_province = no
			has_country_flag = gene_pillars_dragon_book_spirits_chosen
		}
		highlight = yes

		add_adm_power = 25
		add_dip_power = 25
		add_mil_power = 25
	}

	option = { # Core not repaired. Just in case I missed a combination of triggers, make sure at least this one is always shown
		name = gene_pillars.937.i

		add_adm_power = 10
		add_dip_power = 10
		add_mil_power = 10
	}
	
	after = {
		gene_pillar_end_expedition_effect = yes
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		clr_country_flag = gene_pillar_dragon_kobold_suppression
	}
}

#Generic event handler
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.1000
	title = gene_pillars.1000.t
	desc = gene_pillars.1000.d
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	hidden = yes

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.1000.a
		trigger = {
			event_target:gene_pillar_exploration_province = {
				aPUI_check_variable = { name = gene_pillar_health value = 1 }
			}
		}
		random_list = {
			100 = { # Again, again, again, again...
				country_event = { id = gene_pillars.1002 }
			}
			10 = { # Purposefully 1/10th the chance of the others
				trigger = {
					NOT = {
						has_country_flag = gene_pillars_visited_nexus_of_realities
					}
				}
				# A nexus of realities
				country_event = { id = gene_pillars.1003 }
			}
			100 = { # A watery grave
				country_event = { id = gene_pillars.1004 }
			}
			100 = { # Of traps and treasure
				country_event = { id = gene_pillars.1005 }
			}
			50 = { # Trap sprung
				country_event = { id = gene_pillars.1006 }
			}
			100 = { # Locked Out
				country_event = { id = gene_pillars.1007 }
			}

				country_event = { id = gene_pillars.1008 }
			}
			100 = { # Lurker in the dark
				country_event = { id = gene_pillars.1009 }
			}
			100 = { # Pillar Meshi
				country_event = { id = gene_pillars.1010 }
			}
			100 = { # Pillars of Eternity

					}

			}
			100 = { # Navigating the Hinuisundews
				trigger = {
					has_country_flag = gene_pillar_is_exploring_level_1_pillar
					event_target:gene_pillar_exploration_province = {
						province_id = 6962
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = gene_pillars.1020 }
			}
			100 = { # Parasitic Hermit Crab
				trigger = {
					has_country_flag = gene_pillar_is_exploring_level_1_pillar
					event_target:gene_pillar_exploration_province = {
						province_id = 6962
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = gene_pillars.1021 }
			}
			100 = { # Metal Nudibranchs
				trigger = {
					has_country_flag = gene_pillar_is_exploring_level_1_pillar
					event_target:gene_pillar_exploration_province = {
						province_id = 6962
					}
				}
				country_event = { id = gene_pillars.1022 }
			}
			100 = { # Hinuibats
				trigger = {

				}
				country_event = { id = gene_pillars.1050 }
			}
			100 = { # Living Gene Mass
				country_event = { id = gene_pillars.1051 }
			}

		}
