	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.1000.b
		trigger = {
			event_target:gene_pillar_exploration_province = {
				NOT = { aPUI_check_variable = { name = gene_pillar_health value = 1 } }
			}
		}
		reduce_stability_or_adm_power = yes
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_got_killed
		gene_pillar_abandon_expedition_effect = { province_notification_event = yes }
	}
}

# Again, again, again, again...
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.1002
	title = gene_pillars.1002.t
	desc = gene_pillars.1002.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # Press onwards!
		name = gene_pillars.1002.a

		gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = { # Try to break down a wall
		name = gene_pillars.1002.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_barbarian_in_party = yes
				gene_pillars_has_fighter_in_party = yes
				gene_pillars_has_warrior_mechanim_in_party = yes
				high_tolerance_troll_race_trigger = yes
				high_tolerance_ogre_race_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		random_list = {
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
			3 = {
				gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # A hidden passage, perhaps?
		name = gene_pillars.1002.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = rogue }
				high_tolerance_dwarven_race_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		random_list = {
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
			9 = {
				gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Be glad I've got extra chalk
		name = gene_pillars.1002.d
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = ranger }
		}
		highlight = yes

		random = {
			chance = 50
			gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = { # Pray for a sign
		name = gene_pillars.1002.e
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_paladin_in_party = yes
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = cleric }
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		random_list = {
			3 = {
				gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = gene_pillars_generic_move_speed_5
					duration = 1825 # 5 years
				}
			}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = gene_pillars_generic_move_speed_5_minus
					duration = 1825 # 5 years
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Use Guidance
		name = gene_pillars.1002.f
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = mage }
			is_estate_divination_level_1_minimum = yes
			has_mana = { amount = 10 }
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		change_mana = { amount = -10 }
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		gene_pillars_advance_progress_bar = yes
	}
}

# A nexus of realities
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.1003
	title = gene_pillars.1003.t
	desc = gene_pillars.1003.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = {
			set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event
			# To make sure it can only happen once per pillar. Checked in the handler event. Cleared at successful expedition end
			set_country_flag = gene_pillars_visited_nexus_of_realities
		}
	}

	option = { # Continue on foot
		name = gene_pillars.1003.a
	}

	option = { # Is that a damestear core?
		name = gene_pillars.1003.b
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_artificer_in_party = yes
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = mage }
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
	}

	option = { # What can possibly go wrong?
		name = gene_pillars.1003.c

		random_list = {
			10 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 }
			}
			35 = { }
			10 = {
				gene_pillars_add_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
				gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
			10 = {
				gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 3 }
			}
			10 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
				gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
			10 = {
				country_event = { # A watery grave
					id = gene_pillars.1004
				}
			}
			10 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = gene_pillars_generic_prestige_1_minus
					duration = 1825 # 5 years
				}
			}
			5 = {
				gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 25 }
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		gene_pillars_advance_progress_bar = yes
	}
}

# A watery grave
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.1004
	title = gene_pillars.1004.t
	desc = gene_pillars.1004.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # Find an airpocket
		name = gene_pillars.1004.a
		trigger = {
			event_target:gene_pillar_exploration_province = {
				check_variable = {
					which = aPUI_gene_pillar_loot_var
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}

		random = {
			chance = 80
			gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = { # Drop some loot!
		name = gene_pillars.1004.b
		trigger = {
			event_target:gene_pillar_exploration_province = {
				check_variable = {
					which = aPUI_gene_pillar_loot_var
					value = 1
				}
			}
		}

		gene_pillars_lose_loot_effect = { amount = 5 }
		random = {
			chance = 20
			gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = { # Cast water breathing
		name = gene_pillars.1004.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				AND = {
					gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = mage }
					is_overall_transmutation_level_1_minimum = yes
				}
				gene_pillars_has_wavesong_mage_in_party = yes
			}
			has_mana = { amount = 10 }
		}
		highlight = yes

		change_mana = { amount = -10 }
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = { # Emergency dinghy, go!
		name = gene_pillars.1004.d
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
			tier_2_artificer_estate = yes
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		add_country_modifier = { # Clear at end of expedition
			name = gene_pillars_generic_artifice_cap_1_minus
			duration = -1
		}

	}

	option = { # Why are we worried?
		name = gene_pillars.1004.e
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				culture_is_lizardfolk = yes
				culture_is_mechanim = yes
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = { # Just keep swimming
		name = gene_pillars.1004.f
		trigger = {
			NOT = { 
				event_target:gene_pillar_exploration_province = {
					check_variable = {
						which = aPUI_gene_pillar_loot_var
						value = 1
					}
				}
			}
		}

		random = {
			chance = 25
			gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		gene_pillars_advance_progress_bar = yes
	}
}

# Of traps and treasure
# You can choose options to take loot up to 5 times, risking failure each time
# Orb of Omniscience increases the chance of success by 2.5% per level
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.1005
	title = gene_pillars.1005.t
	desc = gene_pillars.1005.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # Leave it for the later survey teams
		name = gene_pillars.1005.a

		custom_tooltip = gene_pillars_generic_extra_reward_at_end_tt
		event_target:gene_pillar_exploration_province = { set_province_flag = gene_pillars_generic_extra_reward_at_end }

		# Reset the counters for next time we encounter this event
		# These are only used if you trigger the A Trap is Sprung event
		hidden_effect = {
			set_variable = {
				which = gene_pillars_generic_traps_and_treasure_loot_gained
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = gene_pillars_generic_traps_and_treasure_xp_gained
				value = 0
			}
			set_variable = {
				which = gene_pillars_generic_traps_and_treasure_count
				value = 0
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = { gene_pillars_advance_progress_bar = yes }
	}

	option = { # Focus on the valuables. Medium loot, small xp
		name = gene_pillars.1005.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = rogue }
				high_tolerance_kobold_race_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		if = { 
			limit = {
				exactly_magic_project_level = { project = orb_of_omniscience level = 1 }
			}
			gene_pillars_generic_loot_or_trap_repeat = {
				success_factor = 825
				fail_factor = 175
				party_loot = 20
				party_xp = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = {
				exactly_magic_project_level = { project = orb_of_omniscience level = 2 }
			}
			gene_pillars_generic_loot_or_trap_repeat = {
				success_factor = 850
				fail_factor = 150
				party_loot = 20
				party_xp = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = {
				exactly_magic_project_level = { project = orb_of_omniscience level = 3 }
			}
			gene_pillars_generic_loot_or_trap_repeat = {
				success_factor = 875
				fail_factor = 125
				party_loot = 20
				party_xp = 1
			}
		}
		else = {
			gene_pillars_generic_loot_or_trap_repeat = {
				success_factor = 800
				fail_factor = 200
				party_loot = 20
				party_xp = 1
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Swift fingers might help. Medium loot, small xp, better success rate
		name = gene_pillars.1005.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = rogue }
				high_tolerance_kobold_race_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		if = { 
			limit = {
				exactly_magic_project_level = { project = orb_of_omniscience level = 1 }
			}
			gene_pillars_generic_loot_or_trap_repeat = {
				success_factor = 925
				fail_factor = 75
				party_loot = 20
				party_xp = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = {
				exactly_magic_project_level = { project = orb_of_omniscience level = 2 }
			}
			gene_pillars_generic_loot_or_trap_repeat = {
				success_factor = 950
				fail_factor = 50
				party_loot = 20
				party_xp = 1
			}
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = {
				exactly_magic_project_level = { project = orb_of_omniscience level = 3 }
			}
			gene_pillars_generic_loot_or_trap_repeat = {
				success_factor = 975
				fail_factor = 25
				party_loot = 20
				party_xp = 1
			}
		}
		else = {
			gene_pillars_generic_loot_or_trap_repeat = {
				success_factor = 900
				fail_factor = 100
				party_loot = 20
				party_xp = 1
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Yes, but knowledge comes first. Small loot, medium xp
		name = gene_pillars.1005.d
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = mage }
				high_tolerance_mechanim_race_trigger = yes
			}
		}

		if = { 
			limit = {
				exactly_magic_project_level = { project = orb_of_omniscience level = 1 }
			}
			gene_pillars_generic_loot_or_trap_repeat = {
				success_factor = 825
				fail_factor = 175
				party_loot = 5
				party_xp = 3
			}
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = {
				exactly_magic_project_level = { project = orb_of_omniscience level = 2 }
			}
			gene_pillars_generic_loot_or_trap_repeat = {
				success_factor = 850
				fail_factor = 150
				party_loot = 5
				party_xp = 3
			}
		}
		else_if = { 
			limit = {
				exactly_magic_project_level = { project = orb_of_omniscience level = 3 }
			}
			gene_pillars_generic_loot_or_trap_repeat = {
				success_factor = 875
				fail_factor = 125
				party_loot = 5
				party_xp = 3
			}
		}
		else = {
			gene_pillars_generic_loot_or_trap_repeat = {
				success_factor = 800
				fail_factor = 200
				party_loot = 5
				party_xp = 3
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # I think I recall these runes. Small loot, medium xp, better success rate
		name = gene_pillars.1005.e
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = mage }
				high_tolerance_mechanim_race_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		if = { 
			limit = {
				exactly_magic_project_level = { project = orb_of_omniscience level = 1 }

				success_factor = 925

				party_xp = 3

		}

# Trap sprung
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.1006
	title = gene_pillars.1006.t
	desc = gene_pillars.1006.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = {
		hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		# Lose all the stuff you gained in the Traps and Treasure event
		while = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = gene_pillars_generic_traps_and_treasure_loot_gained
					value = 1
				}
			}
			change_variable = { gene_pillars_generic_traps_and_treasure_loot_gained = -1 }
			gene_pillars_lose_loot_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
		while = {
			limit = {
				check_variable = {
					which = gene_pillars_generic_traps_and_treasure_xp_gained
					value = 1
				}
			}
			change_variable = { gene_pillars_generic_traps_and_treasure_xp_gained = -1 }
			gene_pillars_lose_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = { # BOOM
		name = gene_pillars.1006.a

		gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 }
	}

	option = { # Cast an emergency ward
		name = gene_pillars.1006.b
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = mage }
			is_estate_abjuration_level_1_minimum = yes
		}
		highlight = yes

		# Level 1 gives you a 50% chance to dodge 1 damage
		# Level 2 gives you a 50% chance to dodge for each point of damage
		# Level 3 avoids damage entirely
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_estate_abjuration_level_2 = yes
			}
			random_list = {
				1 = { }
				2 = {
					gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
				}
				1 = {
					gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_estate_abjuration_level_1 = yes
			}
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
				}
				1 = {
					gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 }
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Dive for cover
		name = gene_pillars.1006.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = rogue }
				high_tolerance_goblin_race_trigger = yes
				high_tolerance_kobold_race_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		highlight = yes

		random_list = {
			1 = { }
			3 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # 'Tis but a scratch
		name = gene_pillars.1006.d
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = fighter }
				gene_pillars_has_flamesong_mage_in_party = yes
			}
		}

		random_list = {
			5 = { }
			35 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
			50 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 2 }
			}
			10 = {
				gene_pillar_injure_random_party_member_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		gene_pillars_advance_progress_bar = yes
	}
}

# Locked Out
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.1007
	title = gene_pillars.1007.t
	desc = gene_pillars.1007.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # Digging it is
		name = gene_pillars.1007.a

		random = {
			chance = 25
			gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_generic_prod_eff_5_minus
			duration = 1825 # 5 years
		}
	}

	option = { # Try to find the missing piece
		name = gene_pillars.1007.b

		random_list = {
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
			}
			3 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = gene_pillars_generic_magic_xp_10_minus
					duration = 1825 # 5 years
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Find the missing piece with MAGIC!
		name = gene_pillars.1007.c
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = mage }
			has_mana = { amount = 10 }
		}
		highlight = yes

		change_mana = { amount = -10 }
		# Base is 50% chance of success, +15% per divination level
		if = {
			limit = {
				is_estate_divination_level_1 = yes
			}
			random_list = {
				65 = {
					gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
				}
				35 = {
					gene_pillars_lose_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = gene_pillars_generic_magic_xp_10_minus
						duration = 1825 # 5 years
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_estate_divination_level_2 = yes
			}
			random_list = {
				80 = {
					gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
				}
				20 = {
					gene_pillars_lose_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = gene_pillars_generic_magic_xp_10_minus
						duration = 1825 # 5 years
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				is_estate_divination_level_3 = yes
			}
			random_list = {
				95 = {
					gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
				}
				5 = {
					gene_pillars_lose_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = gene_pillars_generic_magic_xp_10_minus
						duration = 1825 # 5 years
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {
					gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
				}
				50 = {
					gene_pillars_lose_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = gene_pillars_generic_magic_xp_10_minus
						duration = 1825 # 5 years
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Improvise a solution
		name = gene_pillars.1007.d
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
		}
		highlight = yes
		
		random_list = {
			50 = {
				gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
			}
			50 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = gene_pillars_generic_art_research_speed_10_minus
					duration = 1825 # 5 years
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Improvise a better solution
		name = gene_pillars.1007.e
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
			gene_pillars_is_at_least_party_level = { level = 2 }
		}
		highlight = yes
		
		if = {
			limit = {
				tier_3_artificer_estate = yes
			}
			random_list = {
				95 = {
					gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
				}
				5 = {
					gene_pillars_lose_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = gene_pillars_generic_art_research_speed_10_minus
						duration = 1825 # 5 years
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				tier_2_artificer_estate = yes
			}
			random_list = {
				80 = {
					gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
				}
				20 = {
					gene_pillars_lose_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = gene_pillars_generic_art_research_speed_10_minus
						duration = 1825 # 5 years
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				65 = {
					gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
				}
				35 = {
					gene_pillars_lose_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = gene_pillars_generic_art_research_speed_10_minus
						duration = 1825 # 5 years
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Finally, entertainment!
		name = gene_pillars.1007.f
		trigger = {
			high_tolerance_dwarven_race_trigger = yes
		}
		highlight = yes
		
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_generic_prod_eff_5
			duration = 1825 # 5 years
		}
	}

	option = { # You call that a door?
		name = gene_pillars.1007.g
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				high_tolerance_orcish_race_trigger = yes
				high_tolerance_troll_race_trigger = yes
				high_tolerance_ogre_race_trigger = yes
				gene_pillars_has_barbarian_in_party = yes
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		
		random_list = {
			9 = {
				gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = gene_pillars_generic_shock_10
					duration = 1825 # 5 years
				}
			}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = gene_pillars_generic_shock_10_minus
					duration = 1825 # 5 years
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Suggest the rubble become light as a feather
		name = gene_pillars.1007.h
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_stonestory_mage_in_party = yes
			has_mana = { amount = 10 }
		}
		highlight = yes
		
		change_mana = { amount = -10 }
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		gene_pillars_advance_progress_bar = yes
	}
}

# Unexpected Journey
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.1008
	title = gene_pillars.1008.t
	desc = gene_pillars.1008.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # Draw lots
		name = gene_pillars.1008.a

		gene_pillar_injure_random_party_member_effect = yes
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_generic_land_morale_5_minus
			duration = 1825 # 5 years
		}
	}

	option = { # Offer knowledge
		name = gene_pillars.1008.b
		trigger = {
			event_target:gene_pillar_exploration_province = {
				aPUI_check_variable = { name = gene_pillar_xp value = 20 }
			}
		}

		random_list = {
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_xp_effect = { amount = 3 }
			}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
			}
			2 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Offer wealth
		name = gene_pillars.1008.c
		trigger = {
			event_target:gene_pillar_exploration_province = {
				aPUI_check_variable = { name = gene_pillar_loot value = 20 }
			}
		}

		random_list = {
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_loot_effect = { amount = 15 }
			}
			1 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
			}
			2 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_loot_effect = { amount = 5 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Praies the fey
		name = gene_pillars.1008.d
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				religion_group = fey_religion
				high_tolerance_ruinborn_race_trigger = yes
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		
		add_dip_power = -50
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_generic_land_morale_5
			duration = 1825 # 5 years
		}
	}

	option = { # Present a copy of Portnamm plays
		name = gene_pillars.1008.e
		trigger = {
			high_tolerance_gnomish_race_trigger = yes
			capital_scope = {
				continent = europe # Cannor
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		
		random_list = {
			25 = {
				gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
			70 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
			5 = {
				gene_pillar_injure_random_party_member_effect = yes
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Perform for them
		name = gene_pillars.1008.f
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				high_tolerance_harpy_race_trigger = yes
				gene_pillars_has_wavesong_mage_in_party = yes
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		gene_pillars_advance_progress_bar = yes
	}
}

# Lurker in the dark
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.1009
	title = gene_pillars.1009.t
	desc = gene_pillars.1009.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # Encircle it and charge!
		name = gene_pillars.1009.a

		if = {
			limit = {
				full_idea_group = offensive_ideas
			}
			random_list = {
				8 = {
					gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
					add_prestige = 10
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = gene_pillars_generic_move_speed_10
						duration = 1825 # 5 years
					}
				}
				2 = {
					gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
					add_prestige = -10
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = gene_pillars_generic_move_speed_10_minus
						duration = 1825 # 5 years
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
					add_prestige = 10
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = gene_pillars_generic_move_speed_10
						duration = 1825 # 5 years
					}
				}
				1 = {
					gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
					add_prestige = -10
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = gene_pillars_generic_move_speed_10_minus
						duration = 1825 # 5 years
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Set up a defensive perimeter
		name = gene_pillars.1009.b

		if = {
			limit = {
				full_idea_group = defensive_ideas
			}
			random_list = {
				8 = {
					gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
					add_army_tradition = 5
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = gene_pillars_generic_fort_defense_10
						duration = 1825 # 5 years
					}
				}
				2 = {
					gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
					add_army_tradition = -5
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = gene_pillars_generic_fort_defense_10_minus
						duration = 1825 # 5 years
					}
				}
			}
		}
		else = {
			random_list = {
				1 = {
					gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
					add_army_tradition = 5
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = gene_pillars_generic_fort_defense_10
						duration = 1825 # 5 years
					}
				}
				1 = {
					gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
					add_army_tradition = -5
					add_country_modifier = {
						name = gene_pillars_generic_fort_defense_10_minus
						duration = 1825 # 5 years
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Set up a trap
		name = gene_pillars.1009.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				high_tolerance_kobold_race_trigger = yes
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = ranger }
			}
		}

		random_list = {
			85 = {
				gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = gene_pillars_generic_hostile_attrition_1
					duration = 3650 # 10 years
				}
			}
			15 = {
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = gene_pillars_generic_hostile_1_bad
					duration = 1825 # 5 years
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = { # Send our own horrors into the dark
		name = gene_pillars.1009.d
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = mage }
			is_estate_conjuration_level_1_minimum = yes
			has_mana = { amount = 10 }
		}
		highlight = yes
		
		change_mana = { amount = -10 }
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = { # Deploy daylight flares
		name = gene_pillars.1009.e
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
			tier_2_artificer_estate = yes
		}
		highlight = yes
		
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_generic_artifice_cap_1_minus
			duration = -1
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		gene_pillars_advance_progress_bar = yes
	}
}

# A Decaying Column
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.1015
	title = gene_pillars.1015.t
	desc = gene_pillars.1015.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # Bugger
		name = gene_pillars.1015.a

		gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = { # Flee NOW!
		name = gene_pillars.1015.b
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_ranger_in_party = yes
			gene_pillars_has_rogue_in_party = yes
			gene_pillars_has_mage_in_party = yes

	}

		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = { # Cure me
		name = gene_pillars.1021.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {

				gene_pillars_has_paladin_in_party = yes

		}
		highlight = yes

		}

#Living Gene Mass
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.1051
	title = gene_pillars.1051.t
	desc = gene_pillars.1051.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.1051.a
		if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					gene_pillars_has_amount_of_archetype_in_party = { amount = 2 archetype = fighter }
					gene_pillars_has_amount_of_archetype_in_party = { amount = 2 archetype = ranger }
					AND = {
						gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = fighter }
						gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = ranger }
					}
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = fighter }
					gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = ranger }
				}
				NOT = {
					gene_pillars_has_amount_of_archetype_in_party = { amount = 2 archetype = fighter }
					gene_pillars_has_amount_of_archetype_in_party = { amount = 2 archetype = ranger }
					AND = {
						gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = fighter }
						gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = ranger }
					}
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 50
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				chance = 50
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.1051.b
		gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.1051.c
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_flamesong_mage_in_party = yes
		}
		highlight = yes
		random = {
			chance = 25
			gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.1051.d
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = rogue }
		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 5 }
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.1051.e
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = mage }
		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
		change_innovativeness = 2
	}

	after = { hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }
}

			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
		}

			random = {
				chance = 25
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.1054.b
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = fighter }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 25
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				chance = 50
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.1054.c
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_flamesong_mage_in_party = yes
		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 5 }
		random = {
			chance = 10
			gene_pillar_injure_random_party_member_effect = yes
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.1054.d
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = cleric }
			NOT = { gene_pillars_has_any_mechanim_in_party = yes }
		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		random = {
			chance = 25
			gene_pillars_add_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.1054.e
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_amount_of_archetype_in_party = { amount = 3 archetype = artificer }
		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 20 }
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		gene_pillars_advance_progress_bar = yes
	}
}

#Gravity Anomaly
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.1055
	title = gene_pillars.1055.t
	desc = gene_pillars.1055.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.1055.a
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		random = {
			chance = 10
			gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.1055.b
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 5 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = rogue }
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
			}
			gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		}
		else_if = {
			limit = {
				OR = {
					AND = {
						gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = rogue }
						NOT = { gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer } }
					}
					AND = {
						gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer }
						NOT = { gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = rogue } }
					}
				}
			}
			random = {
				chance = 10
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				chance = 25
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.1055.c
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				culture_group = harpy
				gene_pillars_has_soarer_mechanim_in_party = yes
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.1055.d
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_amount_of_archetype_in_party = { amount = 2 archetype = artificer }
		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.1055.e
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = rogue }
		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 15 }
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		gene_pillars_advance_progress_bar = yes
	}
}

	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province

		name = gene_pillars.1056.a

			chance = 25

		}
	}

		name = gene_pillars.1056.b
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		if = {
			limit = {
				gene_pillars_has_archetype_in_party = { archetype = rogue }
			}
			random = {
				chance = 10
				gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
			}
		}
		else = {
			random = {
				chance = 50

		}

		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 5 }
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.1056.d
		trigger = {
			OR = {
				culture_group = harpy
				gene_pillars_has_soarer_mechanim_in_party = yes
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 1 }
		add_prestige = 5
	}

	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.1056.e
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_stonescrawl_mage_in_party = yes
			has_mana = { amount = 5 }
		}
		highlight = yes
		change_mana = { amount = -5 }
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		gene_pillars_advance_progress_bar = yes
	}
}

#Fabricator

country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.1057
	title = gene_pillars.1057.t
	desc = gene_pillars.1057.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # Gold!
		name = gene_pillars.1057.a
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 20 }
	}

	option = { # Food.
		name = gene_pillars.1057.b
		gene_pillars_add_hp_effect = { amount = 1 }
	}

	option = { # Precursor Steel.
		name = gene_pillars.1057.c
		gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 }
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 15 }
	}

	option = { # Strange Gene Mass.
		name = gene_pillars.1057.d
		random_list = {
			3 = {}
			1 = { gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 } }
		}

		change_innovativeness = 5
	}

	option = { # Try to disassemble the device so we can retroengineer it.
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_amount_of_archetype_in_party = { amount = 2 archetype = artificer }
		}
		highlight = yes
		name = gene_pillars.1057.e
		random_list = {
			3 = {}
			1 = { 
				add_country_modifier = {
					name = gene_pillars_generic_prod_eff_10
					duration = 3650
				}
			}
		}
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		gene_pillars_advance_progress_bar = yes
	}
}

# Mechanim Graveyard
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.1058
	title = gene_pillars.1058.t
	desc = gene_pillars.1058.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # Scrap them.
		trigger = { 
			NOT = { culture_group = mechanim }
			NOT = { culture_is_insyaa_native_country = yes }
		}
		highlight = yes
		name = gene_pillars.1058.a
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 }
	}

	option = { # This is unsettling...
		trigger = { culture_is_insyaa_native_country = yes }
		highlight = yes
		name = gene_pillars.1058.b
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_generic_stab_cost_10
			duration = 1825
		}
	}

	option = { # This is horifying...
		trigger = { culture_group = mechanim }
		highlight = yes
		name = gene_pillars.1058.c
		add_country_modifier = {
			name = gene_pillars_generic_stab_cost_25
			duration = 1825
		}
	}

	option = { # Attempt a miracle
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_amount_of_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer amount = 2 }
			OR = {
				culture_group = mechanim
				culture_is_insyaa_native_country = yes
			}
		}
		highlight = yes
		name = gene_pillars.1058.d
		event_target:gene_pillar_exploration_province = {
			add_mechanim_minority_size_effect = yes
		}
		if = {
			limit = { culture_group = mechanim }
			add_stability_or_adm_power = yes
		}
	}

	option = { # Extract valuables from the machines
		trigger = {
			gene_pillars_has_amount_of_archetype_in_party = { archetype = artificer amount = 2 }
			NOT = { culture_group = mechanim }
			NOT = { culture_is_insyaa_native_country = yes }
		}
		highlight = yes
		name = gene_pillars.1058.e
		gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 15 }
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		gene_pillars_advance_progress_bar = yes
	}
}

# Potions
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.1059
	title = gene_pillars.1059.t
	desc = gene_pillars.1059.desc
	picture = GENE_PILLAR_SPIRIT_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes
	goto = gene_pillar_exploration_province
	trigger = { # Make sure you are still exploring i.e. the party hasn't been wiped
		is_exploring_any_gene_pillar = yes
	}

	immediate = { hidden_effect = { set_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event } }

	option = { # Leave them
		name = gene_pillars.1059.a
		add_prestige = -1
	}

	option = { # Red.
		name = gene_pillars.1059.b
		random_list = {
			1 = { gene_pillars_add_hp_effect = { amount = 1 } }
			1 = { gene_pillars_lose_hp_effect = { amount = 1 } }
		}
	}

	option = { # Blue.
		name = gene_pillars.1059.c
		random_list = {
			1 = { change_mana = { amount = 25 } }
			1 = { change_mana = { amount = -25 } }
		}
	}

	option = { # Green.
		name = gene_pillars.1059.d
		random_list = {
			1 = { gene_pillars_add_xp_effect = { amount = 2 } }
			1 = { gene_pillars_lose_xp_effect = { amount = 2 } }
		}
	}

	option = { # Yellow.
		name = gene_pillars.1059.e
		1 = { gene_pillars_add_loot_effect = { amount = 10 } }
		1 = { gene_pillars_lose_loot_effect = { amount = 10 } }
	}

	after = {
		hidden_effect = { clr_country_flag = gene_pillars_has_pending_event }
		gene_pillars_advance_progress_bar = yes
	}
}

###Debug only event
country_event = {
	id = gene_pillars.99999
	title = gene_pillars.99999.t
	desc = gene_pillars.99999.d
	picture = GOOD_WITH_MONARCH_eventPicture
	
	is_triggered_only = yes

	#Unlock all classes
	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.99999.classes
		
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_fighter_A
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_fighter_B
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_fighter_C
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_fighter_D
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_fighter_E
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_ranger_A
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_ranger_B
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_ranger_C
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_ranger_D
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_ranger_E
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_rogue_A
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_rogue_B
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_rogue_C
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_rogue_D
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_rogue_E
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_cleric_A
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_cleric_B
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_cleric_C
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_cleric_D
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_cleric_E
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_mage_A
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_mage_B
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_mage_C
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_mage_D
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_mage_E
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_artificer_A
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_artificer_B
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_artificer_C
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_artificer_D
		set_country_flag = gene_pillars_unlocked_artificer_E
	}

	#Unlock all party slots
	option = {
		name = gene_pillars.99999.maxparty
		set_variable = {
			which = aPUI_gene_pillars_party_level_var
			value = 5
		}
		gene_pillars = {
			limit = { owned_by = ROOT }
			set_variable = {
				which = aPUI_gene_pillars_party_level_var
				which = PREV
			}
			# set_variable = { which = aPUI_gene_pillar_party_slot_framevar_1 value = @empty }
			set_variable = { which = aPUI_gene_pillar_party_slot_framevar_2 value = @empty }
			set_variable = { which = aPUI_gene_pillar_party_slot_framevar_3 value = @empty }
			set_variable = { which = aPUI_gene_pillar_party_slot_framevar_4 value = @empty }
			set_variable = { which = aPUI_gene_pillar_party_slot_framevar_5 value = @empty }
		}
	}
}
